Iesu abim detager, Ese ma lagelag debele kemerkemer, mara tonar ma bakeam a ko terapei gaire mara lu, ma uiabi nakuarare gaire lu kak le, iaueakai mara lu nagri kotor ge gaire debe lu giz, a ma tabakeam, kari narmili.
Ege abele makeriam asoli abele mer, E adem bakeam au okasosok; abelelam gaire abara lu.
Iesu detager abara kaimeg giz, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Au beber lu giz ra apu a bao kotor baselaia ge.
Kaka uabi detager, Kamela umele bao abele nila neb ge, epe lu giz ra apu umer kak erdali Ade ra baselaia.
Abara kaimeg giz aserare, a uiaba aukase damred, a uiaba mer, kega, Ese mokakalam, nete le umele eded?
Iesu uiabi dasmer, a uiabi detager, Le giz umer kak abele lu; epe Ade umele gaire lu uridili.
Ege Peteru de abim detaut, kega, Dasmer, keriba dikaer gaire lu uridili, a keriba mari narmili; nalu keriba lu nagri?
Ege Iesu uiaba detager, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Uaba kari narmili, ese Le la Uerem egimuru taba opole bao ge a zorom ge, abele ko ditimedlu, a uaba ko bagiri opole bao ge tuelf, a mer atager Isaraela ra nosik tuelf.
Ese nerute le dikaer meta, pako keimer giz, a berbet giz, pako aba, a apu, pako kosker, a omasker giz, a ged giz, kara neilam, E nagri dordor gaire lu mokakalam netate handed, a ko nagri eded aseamur kak.
A gaire le kekiam, a ko keubu; a uader le keubu, a ko kekiam.
Abelelam kotor baselaia abkoreb nerute tarim le, kebi gerger E bakeam a mer atager uader le ikeli abara uina gedub, a ko uiabi bodomalam.
E uiabi detager uader le dorge ikerare netate gerger a netate denari, E uiabi namarkare abara uina gedub.
Abele thri haua ge, E bakeam a ko erdali uader le bako abele zekur uteb, a nole dorge kak;
E uiabi detager, Ua ko bakeuare abele uina gedub, a kaka uabi daisuerare lu abkoreb. Ege uiaba ko bakeuare.
E ko bakeam abele sikis haua ge, pako nain haua, E ko ikeli mokakalam.
Abele ten haua, pako eleuen E ko bakeam, E ko erdali uader le bako a nole dorge kak; E uiabi detager, Nalugem uaba bako ike abele gerger kemerkemer, a nole dorge kak?
A uiaba abi detagerare, Nole le keribi detager. E uiabi detager, Ua ko bakeuare abele uina gedub, a uaba nagri lu abkoreb.
Ege kikem tabarki, abele tarim le abara uina gedub E detager abara sirdam memeg le, Dabgerare gaire gedub le, ma uiaba nakuarare uiaba bodomalam, ditimedilu keubu le ge, a bakedilu kekiam le ge.
Uiaba tabakeuare uader le ditimedilu abele ten haua, pako eleuen haua ge, uiaba nagri netate denari.
Ege kekiam le tabarkare, a uiaba dikiaporare uiaba lu aule nagri; a uiaba netate denari ko daragri.
Uiaba erdarare abele, uiaba mude mer darameare abele tarim le,
Kega, Netate abele haua ge uiaba keubu le dorge, a ma abkoreb uiaba lu keriba lu, keriba au asiasi abele dorgelam, pako abele gereger au urueri.
E detager abele nerute uiabielam a abi kega, Makanali, nole kara adud tonar marim; nako meriba nole mer atager abele netate denari?
Ma ekao mabara lu, ma bakeam; kara dikiapor peike kaka ko ikuar keubu le, mokakalam kaka mari ikuar.
Nako kaka nole karbabu sirdam karbara lu? Nako ma kari op ausiausi kara nase marim?
Mokakalam uader le kekiam a ko keubu, a uader keubu le a ko kekiam. Abelelam gaire le uridili aserare, a neis le mamor epei.
Iesu ogi bakeam Ierusalemaem, E ais abara kaimeg giz tuelf le, abele gab ge uiaba tepteb, E uiabi kega,
Dasmer, meriba ogi Ierusalemaem; a ko namarid Le la Uerem abele au zogozogo le giz pako aotale giz; uiaba abi dedkoare a ko eumilu,
Uiaba abi namarid uiabim gaire nogle, iaueakai uiaba abi neg degarare, pako damerik, a ko abi satauroem: E ko eded akaida thri gerger.
Ege abi tabaruk uiaba apu Zebedaio ra uerem okakis abara neis kimiar uerem, a abi etkobeilu, a damosdare nerute lu.
E abim detager, kega, Nalu lu ma laglag? E abim detaut, Ma uiabi daratager neis kara uerem emeri mari dog, nerute le mara tuter pek, a nerute le mar ber pek, mara baselaia ge.
Ege Iesu etkalu, a uiabi kega, Uaba umer kak abele lu ua kari namosi. Nako uaba umele ereli abele tanelu kaka are, a ko bapatiso abele kari bapatiso ge? A neis le abim kega, Keriba umele.
E uiabi daratager, Uaba ereli kara tanelu, a ko bapataiso kara bapatiso; epe abele le emeri kara tuter pek, pako kara ber pek, nole kara dorge abi ikuar, a uader le kara Aba nakuarare abkoreb uiaba emetu derser.
Uiaba ten le aserare, uiaba nerkep au uekueku abele neis le.
Ege Iesu uiaba dabgerare, E uiabim kega, Ua umele gaire nogle uiaba tarim le nagri E uiabi asesered, a uader aule uiabi tumge E uiabi sirdam.
Uaba nole mokakalam; ese le uaba lagelag aule, debele E uaba memeg le;
Ese le uaba lagelag esaimer, E uaba sorge ekase;
Mokakalam Le la Uerem nole tabarki memeg le taraisare, a E uiaba memeg le, a ko ikuar abara eded bodomalam gaire le giz.
Uiaba osmed Ierikolam, gaire le lakub abi irmilare.
Dasmer, neis le pone asadamer emrilei abele gab ge, a uiaba aserei Iesu tabakeam, uiaba ereretikri, kega, Opole ae, Dauida ra uerem, ma keribi omare.
Ege gaire le lakub uiabi daraisumdarare: epe neis le au ereretikri, kega, Opole ae, Dauida ra uerem, ma keribi omare.
Ege Iesu ekueilu, a darabgere neis le, E uiabi kega, Nalu lu uaba lagelag kaka uabim ikeli?
A ui ge abi detagerei, Opole ae, keriba pone bakaerti.
Ege Iesu au nasenase, a natutilu uiaba pone: ege sobkak ui ge pone bakaerti, a ui ge abi irmilei.
Uiaba maike Ierusalema, a bosi Bethefage, abele Oliua paser, ege Iesu namariklu neis tabara kaimeg giz,
A kega, Ua bakeamlam abele uteb uaba opem, ege uaba sobkak erdali abele asina didbarda, abara uerem okakis: a uaba uiaba detue, a karim tegared.
Ese nerute le uabi nerute mer detager, a uaba abi detager, Opole lagelag; E sobkak uabi ikuar.
Epe gaire lu uridili ikerare, iaueakai bakedilu abele perofeta ra mer, kega,
Uaba abi detagerare Siona ra neur uerem, Dasmer, mara Opole marim tabarki, E gebegeb tonar, E egimulu abele asina, a abara uerem ko.
Ege neis abara kaimeg giz bekeamulei, a ko ikeli mokakalam Iesu uiabim mer tigri;
Ui ge dagaretlei abele asina pako abara uerem, a uiaba am uali dikmerikare abi sor ge, a Iesu ko egimulu.
Abele gaire le lakub uiaba am uali esegarare abele gab ge, a uader le isemar lu tam, a esegarare abele gab ge.
Abele gaire le lakub uader le kekiam pako uader le irmili, a uiaba ereretikri, kega, Hosana abele Dauida ra Uerem: Mapodan le tabarki Opole ra nei, Hosana gaire lu tumge.
E bosi Ierusalema, abele uteb uridili boro, a mer kega, Nete le dali?
Ege le lakub uiaba kega, Abele Iesu ike, Nazareta perofeta, Galilaialam.
Iesu bao Ade ra zogo meta ge, E namuare uridili adige gaire le lu terarpeirare abele zogo meta ge, a erasigilu laulau uader le mani bodomalam, pako sik uader le dibadib bodomalam;
E uiabim detager, Emetu detali, Kara meta nei atker esorerapare meta; a uaba ikerare mokakalam baker kur ge eruam le giz.
Ege abim tabakeuare abele zogo meta ge, uader le pone asamasam, pako uader le ibibi; E uiabi nadgirare.
Gaire au zogozogo le giz pako aotale giz a uiaba erdali abara adigir E ikeli, a kebile giz ereretikri abele zogo meta, kega, Hosana abele Dauida ra Uerem; ege uiaba au uekueku,
Ege uiaba abim kega, Nako ma asoli uiaba mer? Ege Iesu uiabi etkalu, Uao; nako uaba nole atager kak, Ma derser uedakiriare gaire sursur uerem giz uiaba telam, pako nano uerem giz?
E uiabi dikaer, a bakeam abele uteblam Bethania tabarki, a emrilu.
Abele kebi gerger E iako takomeda abele utebim, E uererege.
E dasmer nerute suke abele gab ge, E tabarki, a erdali a nole lu kak abi dog, no lam tepteb; E abim kega, Ma nole ko omeid mara turum niai karem. Epe abele suke sobkak uatuet.
Abara kaimeg giz uiaba erdali a uiaba abi damerare, a mer kega, Nako abele suke ike keserkeser ekeamud?
A Iesu uiabi detager, kega, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Ese uaba oituli, a nole asared kak, uaba ko ikerare nole abele lu suke tepteb, epe ese uaba detagerare abele paser, Ma agisi ma ko bataueret abele gur ge, E umele bakeam.
Gaire lu uridili uaba karim damosare abele esoreraparlam, a oaturlam nagri, uaba ko nagri.
E balu abele zogo meta, a ereuerem, E abim tabakeuare au zogozogo le giz pako aule giz abele ged ge, a uiaba mer, kega, Nalu abele sirdam ma ikeli gaire lu? Nete le marim ikuar abele sirdam?
Ege Iesu uiabim etkalu, kega, Kaka uabi itimer netat mer, ese uaba kari etomeret, a kaka ko uabi etomeret abele sirdam gaire lu kaka ikeli.
Nako Ioane ra bapataiso nagelam? nako kotorlam, nako lelam? Ege uiaba mer atager, kega, Ese meriba daratager, kega, Kotorlam; ege E meribim detager, Nalugelam uaba nole oatur kak abim?
Ese meriba abi detagerare, Lelam; meriba geum gaire le lakub; abelelam uiaba uridili dikiaporare Ioane E perofeta.
Ege uiaba Iesuim etkalu, kega, Keriba umer kak. E uiabim detager, Kaka umer kak uabi etomeret abele sirdam kaka ikeli gaire lu uridili.
Nako uaba dikiapor? Nerute le neis abara uerem; E bakeam abele narbet uerem, a abim kega, Makanali ma bakeam peirdi abele gerger kara uina gedub dorge ikeli.
Ege E abim etkalu, kega, Kaka nole lakak; keubu ko obazgeda, E bakeam.
E ko bakeam nerute uerem, a abara netat mer mokakalam, Ege E abim etkalu, kega, Opole ae, Kaka umele bakeam; epe no mer, a nole bakeam.
Nete le neis uerem ikeli taba aba ra lag? Ege uiaba abim kega, Narbet uerem. Ege Iesu uiabim etkalu, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Kekiam telona giz pako gab kosker giz abele Ade ra baselaia ge bardare, a uaba keubu.
Abelelam Ioane kekiam uabim tabarki barkak tonar ra gab, ege uaba nole abi oatur kak; ege gaire telona giz pako gab kosker giz abi egardare; a uaba umele erdali, a uaba nole keubu obazged, ueakai abim oituli.
Uaba aserare nerute mer babisdarie: Nerute tarim le, E ikeli tabara uina gedub, E kar dirumed, a daiui abele uteb uina detager, a ko ikeli au kar, E uiabim nakuarare gaire uina gedub le, E bakeam muriz gedim.
Maike nur abi, E uiabim namarkare abara memeg le giz uiaba uina gedub le, ko taraisare gaire uina turum.
Ege uiaba gaire uina gedub le erpeirare abara memeg le giz, uiaba damarka nerute, a ipit eumilu nerute, a nerute le uiaba baker erborare.
E uader memeg le ko namarkare gaire le keubu, mokakalam a neis neis memeg le kekiam: a uiaba ko dedkolare uiabim.
Epe keubu E namarid tabara uerem uiabim, E dikiapor, kega, Uiaba geum kara uerem.
A gaire uina gedub le uiaba erdali abara uerem, ege uiaba mer atager, Abara kesem peike; tabakeuare meriba abi ipit eumilu, iaueakai meriba ais abara ged.
Ege uiaba abi erpeirare a ko batauerd adige uina gedublam, epe uiaba abi ipitare eumilu.
Dasmer, ese opole tabarki, E ged kem le, nalu lu ikeli uiabim gaire uina gedub le?
Ege uiaba abi detagerare, E aukase narsare gaire le adud tonar, E ko nakuarare abele uina gedub uader le ko dorge ikerare, a uiaba abi ikuarare turum gaire urut.
Iesu uiabi detager, Nako uaba nole etag abele jauali zogo, Abele baker gaire meta tonar le desauersili, a dikri, a mena ko ikeli kop tumge; abele lu Opole ikeli, meriba dasmerare, a abi damreda?
Abelelam kaka uabi detager, Ade ra baselaia ais adem uabielam, a ko nakuar nerute ged, ueakai tais abara turum.
Ese le abi tumgeabele baker abara lidi erpei: epe abele le baker abi tumge, E mogmog a diskimir.
Au zogozogo le giz pako Faresaio giz aserare abara mer babisdarie, a uiaba opasereret uiabielam Iesu detager.
Ege uiaba lagelag abi erpeirare, a uiaba geum lekublam, abelelam uiaba dikiaporare E perofeta dali.
Ege Iesu ko etomeret uader mer babisdarie uiabim, kega,
Kotor baselaia abkoreb nerute opole, E derser leuer sererege tabara uerem,
E namarkare tabara memeg le uiabim gaire le emetu aserare abele mer tigri, Ua tabakeuare leuer aroem; a uiaba nole lakak tabakeuare.
E ko namarkare uader abara memeg le, a mer kega, Dasmer, kaka emetu derser gaire leuer; kara kau emetu ipitare, a gaire ebur debe kemkem narsare, kaka emetu derser gaire lu uridili, ua tabakeuare leuer aroem.
A uiaba baokarid, a uiaba keubu bamarkare, nerute le tabara ged, a nerute le tabara lu bodomalam;
A uader le uiaba erpeirare abara memeg le, a uiaba dedkolare, pako ipit eumilu.
Abele opole asoli E au urker, E uiabi namarkare gaire tabara ares le, uiaba narsare gaire le dedkolare abara memeg le, a ko digeare uiaba uteb.
E uiabim detager tabara memeg le, Emetu derser leuer, a nole abkoreb uiaba le emetu mer namarid.
Dasmer, uaba bakeuare gaire au gab, a gaire le uridili uaba erdali, uaba etomeret abele leuer.
Ege abara memeg le tabakeuare gaire au gab, a uiaba etami uader le, adud a uader le debele; abele leuer uteb mitkar lelam, uiaba eidi leuer eroare.
Abele opole tabalu abele meta, E uiabi dasmer uiaba eidi leuer eroare, E erdali nerute le nole nagri am uali abkoreb leuer aro am uali;
E abim detaut, Makanali ae, nalugelam ma tabakeam badare abele meta, ma nole nagri abele leuer aro am uali? Ege E nole mer kak.
Abele opole abi detager tabara memeg le, Uaba didbare abara teter pako abara tag, abi ais batauered adige abele kupikup ge; nagri au ebazuer pako abele tereg ikupamaretlare.
Abelelam uader le no aserare, a neis neis le mamor irmilare.
Ege Faresaio giz tabakeuare, a uiaba mer atager, Nalu lu meriba abi mirem abi merlam?
A uiaba namarkare abim uiaba kaimeg giz kemem pako Herodiano giz, abi kega, Ereuer le ae, keriba umele ma le ageakar, mama ereuerem Ade ra gab pako ageakar, ma nole geum nerute le: abelelam ma nole dikiapore nerute le.
Dasmer, ma keribi etomeret, Nako ma dikiapor? Abkoreb ko ikuar Kaisaraim zegu lu, a nole?
Iesu opasereret uiaba nerkep adud, a uiabi kega, Uaba bes le giz, nalugelam uaba kari mirem?
Kari natomertare mani abele zegu lu. Ege uiaba abi ikuar nerute denari.
E uiabi detager, Nete ra op abele, pako abele jauali?
A uiaba abi detagerare, Kaisara ra op. Ege E uiabi detager, Dasmer, Kaisara ra lu Kaisaraim ikuar; Ade ra lu Adim ikuar.
Uiaba aserare, epe uiaba au kase damereda, a uiaba abi dikaer, a adem bakeuare.
Peike abele kerker Sadukaio giz abim tabakeuare, uiaba dikiaporare nole le ko eded akaid eudelam: uiaba abi itimerare,
Kega, Ereuer le ae, Mose keribi mer tigri, Ese eumilu nerute le, a nole uerem kak, abara keimer ko ispi abara kosker, iaueakai nagri kusi abi keimerlam.
Keribi dog emri sefen gaire uerem: a narbet uerem ispi abara kosker, E eumilu a nole uerem kak, abara keimer ko ispi abara kosker:
Mokakalam nerute keimer, mena bakedida sefen le giz.
Abele kosker keubu eumilu.
Dasmer, ese keubu gerger tabarki, nete le uiabielam ais abele kosker? abelelam uiaba kosker uridili.
Ege Iesu etkalu uiabim, kega, Uaba didmirik, abelelam uaba asmer kak abele jauali zogo, pako Ade ra adigir.
Abelelam keubu gerger tabarki uiaba ko eded akaida eudlam, nole kosker aspili kak, a nole kimiar aspili kak, uiaba mokakalam Ade ra angela giz kotor ge.
Abele ko eded akaida eudlam, nako uaba nole atager kak Ade ra mer uabim, kega,
Kaka Aberahama ra Ade, a Isaaka ra Ade, a Iakobo ra Ade? Abele Ade nole eud le giz ra Ade, epe mamor eded le giz.
Gaire lekub aserare, ege uiaba abi damreda abara giz merlam.
Gaire Faresaio giz aserare Sadukaio le nole abi mer kak, ege uiaba etamiare abele uteb ge.
Ege nerute uiaba gelar ereuer le, abi itimer mirem kega,
Ereuer le ae, na gelar aule?
Ege Iesu abi etkalu, Ma abi omare abele Opole mara Ade mara nerkep kemerkemer, a mara lamar kemerkemer, a mara akiapor kemerkemer.
Abele gelar kekiam, pako aule.
Mokakalam abara neisem, Ma abi omare abele le emri mai kesi, mokakalam ma omare mabu.
Peike neis gelar giz abele gelar uridili, pako abele gaire perofeta giz.
Faresaio giz netate gedim, ege Iesu de uiabi nautumerare,
Kega, Nako uaba dikiaporare abele Keriso? nete ra uerem? Ege uiabi abi detagerare, Dauida ra Uerem.
E uiabi detager, Dasmer, Nako Dauida nei atker Lamarlam, E abara Opole, kega,
Abele Opele abi detager kara Opole, Ma emri kara tuter tag, mena kaka ikeli uader le marim kurabkurab mokakalam lu detager mara teter?
Dasmer, ese Dauida E nei atker Opole, a nalugelam E ko nei atker abara uerem?
Ege nole nerute le umele abim etkalu, a ditimedlu abele gerger nole nerute le ko saserim itimer abim nerute lu.
Ege Iesu detager gaire le lakub, pako abara kaimeg giz,
Kega, Aotale giz pako Faresaio giz bakiri Mose ra bas.
Peike uaba mamor asarare a uaba ikerare lu uridili uiaba daratagerare, mamor asarare: epe uaba nole ereuerem uiaba tonar giz; abelelam uiaba no mer detaut, a umer kak ikerare abkoreb.
Abelelam uiaba didbare au lu beber uiaba dikemerik le giz uiaba tabo ge; ege uiaba umer kak uiaba kebi kei etadmir.
Gaire uiaba dorge uridili ikerare, iaueakai le giz uiabi darasmerare: uiaba ikerare au filakteri, pako ko au sisero uiaba am uali,
Uiaba au sererege eidi abele aule ra uteb leuer ero, pako aule ra bao sunago ge,
Pako gaire le uiabi nasege segur uteb ge, a gaire le giz uiaba nei natkerauem, Rabi ae, Rabi ae.
Ege uaba nole nei atker Rabi; abelelam netate uaba Ereuer le, abele Keriso idali, a uaba uridili keimer giz.
Uaba nole nerute le geseb ge nei atker uaba aba; abelelam netate uaba Baba, penoka dali kotor ge.
Uaba nole nei atker ereuer le, abelelam netate uaba Ereuer le, Keriso idali.
Epe abele le aule uabim, E uabim memeg le.
Ese nerute le tababu babei E aule, E ekekeli; Ese nerute le E tababu gebgeb, E bataili uiabim tumge uridili.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! abelelam uaba dimi abele kotor baselaia lelam; abelelam uaba umer kak barot, a uaba ko daraisumdarare uader le barota.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! abelelam uaba ais eseamulu mai kosker uiaba meta, a uaba esorerapare au pereper ikerare ispilu; abele lulam Ade ra urker aule uabi tumge.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! abelelam uaba deraueili gur ge pako sep ge iaueakai uaba nagri nerute le uaba esorerapare; ese uaba erpei, a uaba ikerare Gena ra le E au adud uabielam.
Uaiai uaba datkimuar sadamer le, a uaba mer, Ese le iskosi abele zogo meta nolea kar, epe le iskosi abele zogo meta ra golo, niaiem peike!
Le giz paim ae, pako sadamer; abelelam nade aule, nako abele golo, pako abele zogo meta zogoem abele golo?
A nerute, Ese le iskosi abele zegu lu bao, nolea kar; epe abele iskosi abele zegu lu abi tumge, niaiem peike.
Le giz paim ae, pako sadamer; abelelam nade lu aule, nako zegu lu, nako bao ge zogoem abele zegu lu?
Dasmer, abele le iskosi abele bao zegu lu, E iskosi gaire lu uridili abi tumge.
Abele le iskosi abele zogo meta, E abi iskosi, pako le emeri muige abele zogo meta.
Abele le iskosi abele kotor ge, E iskosi Ade ra bao, pako le abi dog egimulu.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! uaba ikuar kebi lu abele mili pako abele aneto pako abele kumina, a gaire au lu uaba ispilu abele gelarlam, abele barkak tonar, pako abele omare, pako abele oituli: abkoreb ikelare lu ike, a nole dikaer lu peike.
Uaba datkimuar sadamer le, uaba dirimid abele lag, a mamor irusere kemerkemer abele kamela.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! uaba dirup abele tanelu ge ra sor pako abele kumeti, epe muige mitkar lu itike pako abele adud tonar giz.
Mama le Faresaio sadamer, mama kekiam dirup muige abele tanelu ge pako abele kumeti, iaueakai ogo kak kemerkemer abele sor ge.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! abelelam uaba mokakalam ao giz, adige au kakekake, debele le dasmer, epe muige mitkar eud le la lid, pako gaire adud lu uridili.
Mokakalam uaba, adige mokakalam barkak tonar le ise gaire le ra opem, epe muige uaba au mitkar abele bes mer pako abele tonar barbar.
Uaiai uaba aotale pako Faresaio, bes le giz! abelelam uaba emoare gaire perofeta uiaba ao, a ko deiriem uiaba ao le barkak tonar giz,
A uaba mer kega, Ese keriba abi dog emri abele kerker keriba aba giz emeret, umer kak keriba okakis uiaba narsare perofeta giz.
Peike abele mer uabu etomeret uabim, uaba omasker gaire le giz narsare gaire perofeta giz.
A uaba ko mitkar abele tonar lu uaba aba giz lam.
Ege uaba tabo, tabo areg ra omasker giz, nako uaba derar abele urker Genaim?
Dasmer abele lu, kaka uabi namarida perofeta giz, pako pardali le giz, pako aotale le giz; uader le uaba narsare, pako satauroem; a uader le uaba damarika uaba sunago, pako deraimerare nerute uteb a nerute uteb;
Iaueakai bakedida uabi dog gaire le giz barkak tonar uiaba mam uabielam emetu epaitered abele geseb ge, ditimedelu Abela ra mam, le barkak tonar, a bakedilu Zakaria ra mam, abele Barakaio ra uerem, uaba ipiti eumid abele kesi zogo meta pako zegu lu bao ge.
Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Gaire lu uridili tabarki tumem abele nosik.
Ierusalema ae, Ierusalema ae, le ipitare gaire perofeta giz, pako baker erboro le giz emetu namarid marim! kaka au lagelag etami mara omasker giz, mokakalam faul akuadare abara omasker muige abara peo, epe uaba nole la kak!
Dasmer, uaba meta dikaertare a ko pisoger nagri.
Abelelam kaka uabi detager, Uaba umer kak kari dasmer, mena keubu uaba kari daratagerare, Uerkab le tabarki Opole ra nei.
Ege Iesu osmelu adem abele zogo metalam, epe abara kaimeg giz abim tabakeuare, a abi etomeret uader gaire meta giz abele zogo meta ge.
A Iesu uiabi detager, Nako uaba nole asmer kak gaire lu uridili? Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Nole nerute baker igi tumem nerute baker, iako uababuare ueseamulu.
E emri abele Oliua paser, ege abara kaimeg giz abim tabakeuare uiaba tepteb, a uiaba kega, Ma keribi detagerare, Na kerker tabarki abele gaire lu? a nalu atamelam ma tabarki, pako abele geseb ra mop?
Ege Iesu etkalu uiabim kega, Mamoro nole nerute le uabi didmirik.
Abelelam gaire le tabarki kara nei ge, kega, Kakanali abele Keriso; uiaba ko didmirik gaire le.
Uaba aserare abele barseda, pako ares ra mer; uaba nole okasosok, abelelam abkoreb bakedida peike gaire lu uridili, a nole tabarki abele mop ge.
Abelelam nerute ged bakeuare barseda nerute ged, pako nerute baselaia a nerute baselaia, iaueakai memeig tabarki pako gim gim a demali nerute uteb a nerute uteb.
Peike gaire lu uridili abele ditimeda gaire lu asiasi.
Ege uiaba uabi namarkare abele asiasi, pako uiaba uabi deres eumida; a gaire ged uridili uabi derar kara neilam.
Abele kerker gaire le asareda, nerute le mirem nerute le, a uiaba ueku uek.
A gaire perofeta bes tabarki, a uiaba didmirik gaire le.
Gaire le la nerkep gebgeb, abelelam au kale omeid abele adud tonar.
Epe abele le niaiem tekue mena bakedida mop ge, E ko eded.
A ko etomeret debe baselaia ra mer gaire ged narid, ko ikeli ageakarem gaire ged narid; iaueakai bakedilu abele mop ge tabarki.
Ese uaba erdali abele derar lu a dedkolare, mokakalam Daniela perofeta detaut, E tekue abele zogo uteb (le etage mamor dikiapor:)
Uaba Iudaia le abele kerker, uaba derar gaire paser:
Abele le meta tumge nole ko tabu bao ais nerute lu tabara metalam:
Abele le sumez ge nole ko akomeda tabara am uali ais.
Uaiai gaire kosker kem kem pako kosker uerem uerem abele kerker!
Uaba esorerapare iaueakai uaba nole derar abele zeru urut, pako abele sabath ge:
Abelelam abele kerker bakedida au asiasi, nole abkoreb ditimeda gaire lu detagem abele geseb ge bakedida, peirdi nole mokakalam keubu gerger.
Ese nole teupai abele kerker, umer kak nerute le eded: epe sobkak eseamud abele kerker uiabielam emetu depegemerdare.
Ese nerute le uabi detager abele kerker, Dasmer, Keriso ike, pako pedali; uaba nole abi asoli.
Abelelam gaire Keriso bes tabarki, pako perofeta bes, uiaba ikerare gaire au atamelam pako adigir; iaueakai didmirik uader le emetu depegemelu, ese umele.
Dasmer, kaka kekiam uabi detomerta.
Iaueakai ese uiaba uabi detager, Dasmer, E penoka sumez ge; uaba nole bakeuare abim: Dasmer, E muige uteb ge, uaba nole uiabi asoli.
Abelelam mokakalam perper bilba abele naiger pek, a ko datki abele ziai pekem; mokakalam Le la Uerem ko tabarki.
Abelelam abele uteb nagri eud le, gaire aeto abi dog.
Ese emetu eseamud abele asiasi abele kerker, ege abele lem au kupikup nole be kak, abele meb nole meb gerib kak, a uer giz nabuda abele kotorlam, kotor ge demali gaire ares lu.
Ege erdali abele kotor ge abele atamelam Le la Uerem: a gaire nosik le abele geseb ge au ebazuer, a uiaba erdali Le la Uerem tabarki gaire baz abele kotor ge, pako abele adigir a au zorom zorom.
E namarkare tabara angela giz pako abele maber au bumer, a uiaba taraisare foa uag peklam uader le emetu depegemelu, ditimeda kotor paikai a bakedilu nerute paikai.
Uaba dikiaporare abele mer babisdarie abele suke; Ese kerkar omeida abara girikupi tam, pako au lamalam; uaba umele urueri urut maike:
Mokakalam uaba, ese uaba erdali gaire lu uridili, uaba umele E maike abele gab te ge.
Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Nole eseamud abele nosik, mena bakedilu gaire lu uridili.
Eseamulu abele kotor ge, pako abele geseb ge, epe kara mer giz nole aseamur kak.
Ege abele kerker pako abele haua ge nole le asmer kak, a angela giz kotor ge nole umer kak, ege kara Aba tepteb.
Mokakalam Noa ra kerker, abkoreb Le la Uerem ko tabarki.
Abelelam mokakalam abele kerker mega ogiri nole tabarki, uiaba eroli a ereli, a uiaba kosker ispida pako namarid, bakedilu abele kerker Noa balu abele tabara nar ge,
A uiaba umer kak abele mega ogiri tabarki, a uiaba uridili ais adem eseamulu; mokakalam Le la Uerem ko tabarki.
Abele kerker neis le emri sumez ge; nerute le ais, a nerute le ikedi.
Neis kosker edatimiri abele uteb saito edatimiri; nerute kosker ais, a nerute kosker ikedi.
Peike, uaba nole ute kak, abelelam uaba umer kak na haua ge uaba Opole tabarki.
Uaba dasmer abele lu, ese tarim le ra boai umele abele haua ge eruam le tabakeam abele ki ge, E umele asesered, E nole dikaer tabara meta ko daiui.
Abele lu uaba mamor derser; abelelam abele haua ge uaba nole akiapor kak, Le la Uerem tabarki.
Nete abele ageakar memeg le pako debe akiapor, abara opole E ikosi a sirdam gaire memeg le, E uiabi ikuar uiaba leuer gaire haua abkoreb?
Uerkab abele memeg le, ese abara opole tabarki, a abi erdali mena ikeli abkoreb.
Ageakar kaka uabi detager, E abi ikosi ko sirdam abara gaire lu uridili.
Ese abele adud memeg le E tababu detager tabara nerkepu, Kara opole uapum tabakeam;
E ipit tabara kaimeg memeg le, a ko eroare pako ereli okakise uader le turtur ereli;
Abele memeg le ra opole tabarki abele gerger nole asesere kak, pako abele haua E nole asmer kak,
E au bodomalam ikuar abim, a ko abi ikuar abara uteb kemem gaire bes le giz; nagri au ebazuer pako tereg ikupamaretlare.
Abele kerker kotor baselaia abkoreb ten gaire neur, uiaba ais uiaba lamepa, a uiaba bakeuare obapit abele le kerkar kosker ispid.
A uiaba faif neur pardali nagri, a faif neur paim paim nagri.
Uader neur paim paim, no lamepa ais, a nole ide kak;
Epe uader neur pardali, uiaba tarpor ide ais kemem lamepa.
Ege au uapum tabarki abele le kerkar kosker ispili, epe uiaba uridili uteid uaepiti a ko uteid.
Eipu ki ge tabarki abele le ereretikri tabarki, Dasmer, abele le kerkar kosker ispili tabakeam, uaba bakeuare abi obapit.
Ege neur uridili bako, a derser uiaba lamepa.
Ege paim paim neur uiaba uiabi daratagerare pardali neur, Uaba keribi ikuar ide; abelelam keriba lamepa maike asameida.
Epe pardali neur uiabi etkalu, kega, Nole abkoreb keribim pako uabim; debele uaba bakeuare uader le lu terapei, ua ko bodomalam uiabim.
Uiaba bakeuare ko bodomalam, epe abele le kerkar kosker ispili tabakeam; uiaba le emetu derser uiaba barota kemem okakis abim abele leuer sererege; ege abele te dimilu.
Keubu uader neur ko tabakeuare, a uiaba kega, Opole ae, Opole ae, ma diski abele te keribim.
E uiabi etkalu, kega, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, kaka nole asmer kak uabim.
Peike, uaba nole ute kak, abelelam uaba umer kak abele gerger pako abele haua ge Le la Uerem tabarki.
Mokakalam nerute le muriz ge bakeam, E darabgerare tabara memeg le giz, E uabi ikuar abara gaire lu.
E ikuar nerute le faif talen, a nerute le neis, a nerute le netat, abkoreb abele gaire lu le umele; epe E bakeamulu.
Abele le faif talen E bakeam ko terapei, E ko nagri uader faif talen.
Mokakalam abele le nagri neis talen, E ko nagri uader neis talen.
Epe abele le nagri netat talen E bakeam a daiui abele seb, a ko ispilu abara opole ra mani.
Gaire ki ge eseamulu abele memeg le ra opole tabarki, a uiaba mer atager abi luglam.
Abele le nagri faif talen E tabakeam a ko tais uader faif talen, a abi kega, Opole ae, ma kari ikuar faif talen; dasmer, kaka ko nagri uader faif talen.
Abara opole abi detager, Au debele abele debe megmeg le ae, pako ageakar; ma ageakar abele uader kebi lu, kaka mari ikosi ko sirdam gaire au lu; ma tabakeam balu abele mara opole ra sererege.
Abele le nagri neis talen E tabakeam a abi detager, kega, Opole ae, ma kari ikuar neis talen; dasmer, kaka nagri uader neis talen.
Ege abara opole abi detager, Au debele abele debe memeg le ae, pako ageakar; ma ageakar uader kebi lu, kaka mari ikosi ko sirdam gaire au lu; ma tabakeam balu abele mara opole ra sererege.
Abele le nagri netat talen E tabakeam a abi detager, kega, Opole ae, kaka erdali mama au peper tonar le, ma ismi abele uteb ma nolea saito tigri, ma ko etami lu abele uteb ma nole depegelu:
Epe kaka au geum, a kaka bakeam ko ispilu mara talen abele seb ge; dasmer, mara lu ike.
Abara opole abi etkalu, kega, Adud memeg le ae, pako au gebgeb, ma umele kaka ismi abele uteb kaka nole saito tigri, a kaka ko etami lu abele uteb kaka nole depegelu:
Peike abkoreb, ese ma ikuar kara mani uader le mani terapei, iaueakai kaka tabakeam ko nagri kara lu pako abara bodomalam.
Dasmer, uaba tais abele talen abielam, a ko ikuar abele le nagri ten gaire talen.
Abelelam, ese le nagri lu, a ko ikuar abim lu, iaueakai au gaire lu abi dog: epe ese le nolea lu kak, debele ais adem abielam abele lu E nagri.
Uaba imud abele memeg le nole abkoreb, abele kupikupi adige, nagri au ebazuer pako tereg ikupamaretlare.
Ese Le la Uerem tabarki tabara zorom, pako zogo angela giz uridili kemem abi dog, epe E egimuru tabara bao zorom ge:
Etami abara opem gaire ged narida uridili; E nakesmulu uiabim, mokakalam le asesered mamoe, E nakesmulu nani, pako mamoe;
Ege ikedi mamoe abara tuter tag, a nani abara ber tag.
Abele Opole uiabi detager uader le abara tuter tag, Uaba tabakeuare uaba emetu kara Aba uabi ikuar debe mer, uaba uteb abele baselaia, emetu derser uabim a nole detagem abele geseb ge:
Abelelam kaka uererge, a uaba kari ikuar leuer kaka eroli; a kaka niap, a uaba kari ikuar ni kaka aree; a kaka supe le, a uaba kari egared:
Kaka nole nesur kak, a uaba kari ikuar am uali; a kaka gimgim, a uaba kari dasmer; kaka emeri abele audubare meta, a uaba tabakeuare kari dasmer.
Barkak tonar le giz uiaba etkalu, kega, Opole ae, na gerger keriba erdali ma uererege, a keriba mari asisiem? pako niap, a keriba mari ikuar ni ma ereri?
Na gerger keriba mari erdali ma supe le, a keriba mari egared? pako nole nesur kak, a keriba mari ikuar am uali?
Na gerger keriba mari erdali ma gimgim, pako ma emeri abele audubare meta ge, a keriba bakeuare mari dasmerare?
Ege Opole uiabi etkalu, kega, Ageakar kaka uabi detager, Abelelam uaba ikerare nerute le kebi kale kara keimer ike, kakanali uaba ikerare.
E uiabi detager uader le abara ber tag, Uaba le adud tonar, bakeuare adem karielam, abele ur niai karem, emetu derser abkoreb abele diabolo pako tabara angela giz:
Abelelam kaka uererege, a uaba nole kari ikuar leuer; a kaka niap, a uaba nole kari ikuar ni kaka aree:
Kaka sup le, a uaba nole kari egared; kaka nole nesur kak, a uaba nole kari ikuar am uali; kaka gimgim, kaka emeri abele audubare meta, uaba nole kari dasmer.
Ege uiaba etkalu abim, kega, Opole ae, na gerger keriba mari erdali ma uererege, pako niap, pako supe le, pako nesur kak, pako gimgim, pako emeri abele audubare meta, a keriba nole mari memege le?
E uiabim etkalu, kega, Ageakar kaka uabi daratagerare, Abelelam uaba nole ikerare nerute le kebi kale uiaba ike, epe kakanali uaba nole ikerare.
Ege uiaba bakeuare peike abele asias niai karem: epe barkak tonar le giz ko bakeuare abele eded niai karem.
Iesu eseamulu abara mer uridili, E uiabi detager tabara kaimeg giz,
Uaba umele, eseamud neis gereger abele paseka ikeli, a Le la Uerem namarid ko satauroem.
Abele kerker etami gaire zogozogo le giz, pako aotale giz, pako aule giz abgedlam abele zogo le ra meta ge, abara nei Kaiafa;
A uiaba mer atager nalu lu umele mirem erpei, pako ipitare eumilu Iesu.
A uiaba kega, Nole ikeli abele uetpur, iaueakai abele ged ataperetlam.
Iesu emri Bethania, Simona lepera ra meta,
Nerute kosker abim tabakeam nagri abele alabasa tarpor, muige abele ide debe lagelag au bodomalam, E epaitered abara kerem, a E eidi leuer aroem.
Abara kaimeg giz uiaba erdali, uiaba nerkepu au asiasi, a uiaba kega, Nalugelam abele lu dedkoli?
Abelelam, ese terapei abele ide debe lagelag, mena gaire lu bodomalam a ko nakuarare gaire lu kak le.
Iesu umele, E uiabi kega, Nalugem uaba bamsili abele kosker? abelelam E debe lu karim ikeli.
Abelelam uaba mena emri okakis gaire lu kak le, epe kakanali uabim nole niai emri.
Abelelam E epaitered abele ide debe lagelag kara gem kekiam, keubu kara etkobei.
Ageakar, kaka uabi detager, Gaire ged uridili abele geseb ge etomertare abele euangelia, a ko etomeret abele lu abele kosker ikele mena ko dikiapor abim.
Nerute le abele tuelf lelam, abara nei Iuda Isakariota, E bakeam gaire au zogozog le giz,
A uiabi kega, Nalu lu uaba kari ikuar, a kaka abi ikuar uabim? Ege uiaba abi ikuar mani thirti.
Abele gerger ge E ditimed mirem abim, na kaua umele ko abi erpei.
Abele kekiam gerger abele areto nole isi kak, abara kaimeg giz Iesuim tabakeuare, a abim kega, Nade uteb ma lagelag keriba derser ko paseka eroare?
Ege E uiabi detager, kega, Uaba bakeuare abele uteb, a nerute le uaba abi daratagerare, Abele Ereuer le mari detager, Kara mop maike; kaka ikeli abele paseka mara meta, kaka pako kara kaimeg giz.
Ege abara kaimeg giz ikerare mokakalam Iesu mer tigri, a ko derser abele paseka.
Kikem tabarki, E eidi leuer ero kemem tuelf le.
Uiaba eroare, E uiabi detager, Ageakar, kaka uabi detager, uabielam nerute le kari mirem.
A uiaba au asiasi, a uiaba ditimeda abim detagerare, Opole ae, nako kaka?
E uiabi etkalu, kega, Abele le kemem akameida abara tag, pako kara tag abele tanelu ge, E dali abele le kari mirem.
Le la Uerem bakeamulu, mokakalam detarer abim; epe abele le Le la Uerem abi mirem uaiai abele le! debele abele le nole aosmer kak.
Ege Iuda, le abi mirem, abi etkalu, kega, Rabi ae, nako kaka? E abi detager, Eko mama detager.
Uiaba eroare, Iesu ekao abele areto, a esoao, a itur; a uiabim nakuarare tabara kaimeg giz, kega, Tekao, aroem; kara gem ike.
E tanelu ekao, a esoao, a uiabim nakuarare, kega, A ui uridili areem;
Abelelam kara mam ike, abele mam kerkar gelar ko epaitered gaire le giz adem dikri le ra uite giz.
Kaka uabi detager, kega, Kaka nole aree kak abele uina turumlam, mena bakedida abele gerger kaka ko aree abele kerkar uaina uabi kemem kara Aba ra baselaia.
Uiaba emetu uedakiriare nerute ued, a uiaba Oliua paserem bakeamuda.
Ege Iesu uiabi detager, Uaba uridili ezigmada karielam abele ki ge; emetu detali, kega, Kai le mamoe asesered ipiti, epe mamoe giz kepu bamarid.
Ese kaka ko eded akaida, kaka kekiam bakeam Galilaiaem, a uaba keubu.
Epe Peteru abi detager, kega, Ese ui uridili marim ezigmada, kai nolea.
Iesu abi detager, kega, Ageakar kaka mari detager, kega, Abele ki ge, kimiar faul nole ereretikri kak, a neis netat ma kari nasared.
Peteru iako elele detager, kega, Ese kaka mari kemem naumilu, kaka nole mari asared kak. Uiaba uridili daratagered abkoreb.
Uiaba baosi kemem Iesu abele ged nei Gethesemane, E uiabi detager, tabara kaimeg giz, Uaba bamer ike, a kaka bakeam peike ko esorerapare.
E bakeuare kemem Peteru pako Zebedaio ra neis uerem, E au asiasi a ko okasosok.
E uiabi detager, Kara nerkepu au asiasi, bakedida abele eud; uaba ko bamer ike, pako kari kemem uti kak.
E kebikebi bakeam, a E etkobeilu, a esorerapare, kega, Kara Aba ae, ese umele, adem abele tanelu karielam; epe nole kara lag ikeli, mabara lag ikeli.
E ko akomed a erdali abara kaimeg giz uiaba uteid, E detager Peteruim, Nako, uaba nole saserim kari kemem uti kak abele netat haua ge?
Uaba uti kak a esorerapare, iaueakai uaba nole mirem barota; merkepu au lagelag, a gem gebegeb.
E iako bakeam, a esorerapare, kega, Kara Aba ae, ese nole umele adem abele tanelu karielam, mena kaka aree, mabara lag ikeli.
E iako akomeda a uiaba erdali ko uteid, abelelam uiaba pone au perper.
E uiabi dikaer, a ko bakeam esorerapare abele neis netat bakeam, E no netat mer detager.
E iako akomeda a erdali abara kaimeg giz, E uiabi kega, Uaba uteid, a nerbazi: dasmer, maike abele haua Le la Uerem ko abi mirem gaire uit le giz ra tag.
Bako, meriba bakeuare: dasmer, E maike abele le kari mirem.
Dasmer, E mer detaut, Iuda tabarki, nerute le tuelf lelam, E kemem gaire le lakub, pako zogozogo le giz, a aule giz abgedlam, uiaba nagri teibur aososo tulik pako gabgab.
Abele le abi mirem E uiabi etomeret nerute atamelam, kega, Abele le kaka abi eskos, E dali: uaba abi erpeirare.
E sobkak tabarki Iesuim, a abi kega, Rabi ae; a abi eskos.
Iesu abi detager, kega, Makanali, nalugem ma tabakeam? A uiaba tabakeuare a tag giz Iesui dog emarirare, a ko erpeirare.
Dasmer, nerute le Iesui dog E ekao tabara teibur aososo tulik iseda, E ipiti nerute zogozogo le giz ra memeg le abara laip ismilu.
Iesu abim detager, Mara teibur aososo tulik ko ikedi taba gedge; abelelam uiaba uridili ekao abele teibur aososo tulik, a ko eumilu abele teibur aososo tuliklam.
Nako ma dikiapor kaka nole umele damosi kara Aba ko namarkare karim gaire angela giz tumem gaire legiona tuelf?
Nako nole bakedida gaire iauali zogo, abkoreb bakedida abele gaire lu?
Peirdi abele haua kige, Iesu detager gaire le lakub, Nako uaba karim tabakeuare, gaire teibur aososo tulik, pako gabgab ko erpei mokakalam idikeda le ise? Meriba bamer abele zogo meta, kaka uabi ereuerem gaire gerger, a uaba nole kari erpei.
Gaire lu uridili ikerare, iaueakai bakedilu gaire perofeta giz uiaba iauali. Abara kaimeg giz abi dikaerti, a uiaba derar.
Uiaba Iesu erpeirare, a abi datkimuardare Kaiafaim zogo le, a gaire aotale giz le pako aule giz netate gedim.
Epe Peteru muriz ge abi irmili, zogo le ra meta tabarki, a balu a emri kemem gaire memeg le, E lagelag erdali abele mop.
Ege gaire zogo le giz pako aule giz pako gaire tarim le uridili uiaba deraimerare uader le bes ageakarem Iesuim, iaueakai uiaba abi ipitare eumilu:
Epe nole erdali; a ko tabakeuare gaire bes ageakarem, a nole ardar kak. Keubu neis le bes ageakarem tabakeamlei, a kega,
Abele le keribi detager, Kaka umele Ade ra zogo meta ezageri, kaka umele ko ikeli neis netate gerger.
Abele zogo le ekue, a abim kega, Nako ma nole mer etkalu? nako neis le ra mer marim?
Epe Iesu nole mer kak. Ege zogo le abim detager, kega, Kaka mari detager, Ma iskosi keribim edede Ad ra nei, nako mama Keriso Ade ra Uerem?
Ege Iesu abi detager, Eko, mama detager; kaka uabi detager, Keubu uaba erdali Le la Uerem E emri tuter tag abele adigir kemer le, E ko tabakeam gaire kotor baz giz ge.
Abele zogo le tabara am uali etoat, a uiabi kega, E adud mer egali Adim: nako, nole ko abkoreb nerute ageakarem meribim? dasmer, uaba aserare peirdi abara adud mer egali Adim.
Nako uaba dikiaporare? Ege uiaba daratagerare, kega, Abkoreb E eumilu.
Ege uiaba mos iduari abara opem; a uader le tag giz ipitare abim,
A uiaba mer kega, Keriso ae, mase keribi etomertare, nete le mari ipiti?
Epe Peteru E adige emri abele meta ge; nerute memeg neur abim tabakeamulu kega, Mama nerute le kemem Iesu Galilaia le.
E abi asared uiaba opem uridili, kega, Kaka umer kak abele lu ma kari detager.
E teosomeda abele maisu ge, a nerute memeg neur ko abi erdali, E detager uader le, Abele le E kemem Iesu Nazareta le.
E ko abi asared, a ditimeda adud mer egali, kega, Kaka umer kak abele le.
Kebikebi, uader le tekueilu, a uiaba kega, Peteruim, Ageakar ma nerute le uiabielam; abelelam keriba umele mara kodomer.
E ko adud mer egali, a iskosi, kega, Kaka umer kak abele le. Ege kimiar faul sobkak ereretikri.
Epe Peteru ko dikiapor abele mer Iesu abi detager, Nole kimiar faul ereretikri kak, ma neis netat kari asared. Ege osomed E au ezoli.
Gerger osakeida, gaire zogozogo le giz uridili, pako aule giz abgedlam uiaba mer atager Iesu ko abi ipit eumilu:
Uiaba abi didbari, ege uiaba datkimoardare a abi ikuar Pontio Pilato abele opole.
Iuda umele, abele le abi mirem, E ko obazgeda, a ko ikuar thirti gaire mani gaire zogozogo le, pako aule giz,
Kega, Kaka au uit le, abelelam kaka mirem abele le nole uit kak. A uiaba abi kega, Nako keribim abele lu? epe ma mabu abele lu.
E batauered abele gaire mani abele zogo meta ge, E adem bakeam; E bakeam a tababu baudubari.
Gaire zogozogo le giz uiaba ekao abele gaire mani, a kega, Abele lu gelar, umer kak ikedilu abele mani uteb ge gaire zogo lu ikedi, abelelam mam bodomalam.
Uiaba mer atager, epe abi bodomalam le ikeli kakekak tanelu ra ged, a ko etkobeilu gaire sup le.
Abelelam nei atker abele ged, Mam ra ged, bakedida peirdi abele gerger.
Iaueakai bakedelu Ieremia perofeta ra mer, kega, Uiaba ekao abele thirti mani, abele le bodomalam, uader Isaraela ra omasker uiaba abi bodomalam;
A uiaba abi bodomalam le ikeli kakekak tanelu ra ged, mokakalam abele Opole uiabi detager.
Iesu ekueilu opole ra opem; abele opole abi itmer, kega, Nako mama Iudaia le giz ra Opole? Iesu abi etkalu, Eko, mama detager.
Gaire zogozogo le giz pako aule giz uiaba abi etomertare gaire abara mer, epe E nole mer kak.
Pilato abi detager, Nako ma asoli gaire lu uiaba mari etomertare?
Epe E nole abi etkalu netate mer; abelelam abele opole au damred.
Opole ra tonar namarid nerute uetpur abele gaire le lakubem nerute le didbari, uiaba lagelag.
Abele kerker uiaba nagri nerute le didbari, au adud le, abara nei Barabasa.
A uiaba netate uteb ge, Pilato uiabi detager, Nete le uaba lagelag kaka uabi namarid? Nako Barabasa? Nako Iesu, le nei atker Keriso?
Abelelam E umele uiaba kurablam abim ikuar.
E egemeru abele mer atager bao ge, abele merkem tabakeam tabara koskerlam, kega, Ma nole abi dedkoli abele le barkak tonar; abelelam kaka au asiasi kara peim abim abele gerger.
Gaire zogozogo le giz pako aule giz uiaba namarkare gaire le lakub uiaba abi daratagerare, Barabasa namarid, a Iesu ipit eumilu.
Abele opole uiabi detager, kega, Nete le neis le peike uaba lagelag kaka uabi namarid? Ege uiaba daratagerare, Barabasa.
Pilato uiabi etkalu, kega, Nalu lu kaka ikeli Iesuim, abele le nei atker Keriso? Ege uiaba uridili abi daratagerare, Abi satauroem.
Opole uiabi etkalu, Nalu adud E ikeli? A uiaba aukase ereretikri, kega, Abi satauroem.
Pilato umele uiaba nole asoli abara mer, a uiaba au sasemi, E ekao abele ni abara tag dirup gaire le lakub ra opem, a uiabi kega, Kaka ogog kak abele barkak tonar le ra mam: uabu abele.
Abele ged uridili abi daratagerare, kega, Keribi tumge, pako keriba omasker giz, abara mam.
E Barabasa namarid uiabielam, E abi damarik Iesu, a ko ikuar abi satauroem.
Gaire ares le uiaba datkimoardare Iesu abele opole ra meta, a uiaba netate gedim abim gaire ares le uridili.
Uiaba iki adem abara am uali, a uiaba abi ame abele mamam am uali.
Uiaba euerare abele aper abele lu zegerzeger, a uiaba dikmerik abi kerem ge, a uiaba ikedirare abele kokeda abi tuter tag ge, a uiaba kokmamu abim, kega, Uaiai abele Iudaia le giz ra Opole!
Uiaba abi mosu iduare, a uiaba edarkare abele kokeda a ko ipitare abi kerem ge.
Uiaba emetu abi neg degarare, a uiaba detueare adem abele am uali, a ko abi ame tabara am uali, ege uiaba abi datkimoardare ko satauroem.
Uiaba bakeuare, a uiaba erdarare nerute Kurene le, abara nei Simona; a uiaba damsare abim ko ais abara satauro.
Uiaba abele utebe tabarki nei atker Gologotha, tonar abele, Kerem lid ra uteb,
Uiaba abi ikuar abele uinega ataperet okakis abele kurab lu E ereri; E kebikebi ere, a umer kak ere.
Uiaba abi satauroem, ege uiaba terapei abara am uali, a luglug ikeli netede ekardare: iaueakai bakedilu abele perofeta ra mer, Uiaba terapeirare gaire kara am uali, a uiaba luglug ikeli kara gem uali.
Uiaba bamer abele utebe abi asesered;
Uiaba dikmerik tumem abi kerem ge abele jauali, abele lu abi emerered, Abele Iesu Iudaia le giz ra Opole.
Uiaba abi satauroem kemem abi dog neis eruam le, nerute le tuter tag, a nerute le ber tag.
Gaire le nakasir, uiaba abi adud mer nakarare, a uiaba kerem abi dirilare,
Kega, Mama le zogo meta ezageri, a neis netat gerger ko ikeli, ma mabu eded. Ese mama Ad ra Uerem, ma mabu tarabu abele sataurolam.
Mokakalam zogozogo le giz, pako aotale giz, pako aule giz, uiaba abi neg degarare a kega,
E umele uader le idigir, a nole umer kak tababu idigir: Ese E dali Isaraela Opole debele E uatabu peirdi abele sataurolam, iaueakai keriba abi oituli.
E Adim oituli; debele peirdi E abi idigir, ese E abi omare: abelelam E detager, kaka Ade ra Uerem.
Mokakalam abele neis eruam le kemem abi dog satauroem, uiaba abi adud mer egali taba opem.
Ditimedlu abele sikes haua kupikupi ged ge uridili bakedilu abele nain haua ge.
Maike nain haua Iesu au ereretikri, kega, Eli, Eli, lama sabakethani? tonar abele, Kara Ad, kara Ad, nalugem ma kari nakaerti?
Uader le bako aserare, ege uiaba kega, E Elia dabgeri.
Nerute le uiabielam E koreder ekao abele sap, a akameilu abele uinega, a agisilu pater ge, a abi ikuar ere.
A uiaba uridili abi daratagerare, Dikaer; meriba dasmer, nako Elia umele tabarki ko abi idigir.
Iesu ko au ereretikri, epe namarid tabara lamar.
Dasmer, abele uali demed zogo meta muige tababu batoat kotorlam a giz ge; abele sep demali; a neide nakesmur;
Gaire ao emetu te diski; gaire zogo le ko eded akaida eudlam;
Emetu abara ko eded akaida, uiaba bakeuare abele zogo uteb, gaire le uiaba dasmerare.
Abele kerem le netate handed nosik le, pako uader le kemem Iesu abi asesered, uiaba erdarare abele sep demali, pako gaire lu ikerare, a uiaba au geum, kega, Ageakar Ade ra Uerem idali.
Gaire kosker giz uiaba muriz ge abi dasmerare, uiaba Iesu abi irmilare Galilaialam, uiaba abi memeg:
Uiabi kemem Maria Magadalena, pako Maria Iakobo a Iose uiaba apu, a Zebedaiora uerem uiaba apu.
Abele kikem tabarki, nerute le lu giz ra apu Arimathia le, abara nei Iosefa, E nerute Iesu ra kaimeg giz:
E bakeamulu Pilatoim abi damos abele Iesu ra gem. Pilato uiabi detager ko abi ikuar abele gem.
Iosefa ais abele gem, a sopem erebe abele uali lino og kak,
A ikedilu tabara ao ge kerkar, E daiui abele neide: E erparik nerute au baker abele ao ra te, E bakeamulu.
Maria Magadalena pako nerute Maria, uaiba emrilei obakuei abele ao ge.
Abele nerute gerger, abele gerger maike abele derser gerger, gaire zogozogo le giz, pako Faresaio giz netate gedim Pilatoim,
Kega, Opole ae, keriba ko dikiaporare abele bes le E emetu detager, Abele kerker eded, eseamud neis netate gerger kaka ko tekue.
Dasmer, ma uiabi detager ko dimilu abele ao, mena bakedilu neis netate gerger, iaueakai nole abara kaimeg giz bakeuare ki ge ko abi eruam, a uiaba ko daratagerare abele ged, E ko tekueilu eudlam; iaueakai au bes keubu, abele kekiam bes.
Pilato uiabi detager, Uaba nagri asesered le; ua bakeuare uabu dimrare.
Uiaba bakeuare, a dimrare abele ao ge, a ikedi atamelam abele baker, a uader le ikedi uiabi asesered.
Sabath eseamulu, baneigiri abele kekiam gerger sefen, Maria Magadalena pako nerute Maria ui bakeamlam abi dasmer abele ao ge.
Dasmer, abele aukase demali: abelelam abele Opole ra angela kotorlam tarabu, E bakeam erbariklu adem abele baker ao telam, E egimulu abi tumge.
Abara op mokakalam perper ise, pako abara am uali au kakakak mokakalam kiona ise:
Uiaba asesered le au geum a durdur barki, uiaba tarbigrare mokakalam eud le giz.
Abele angela uiabi detager neis kosker, kega, Uaba nole geum kak; abelelam kaka umele uaba deraimer Iesu le, emetu satauroem.
E nole ike, abelelam E ko eded akaid, mokakalam E detager. Ua tabakeamlam abi dasmeram abele uteb abele Opole emetu uteid.
Ua bakeamlam dudum etomeret abara kaimeg giz, E akaid eudelam; dasmer, E kekiam bakeamulu Galilaiaem, uaba keubu; uaba ko abi erdali abele uteb: dasmer, kaka etomeret uabim.
Ui bakeamlei dudum abele aolam, ui geum a au sererege; a koreder etomeret abara kaimeg giz.
Ui bakeamlei etomeret abara kaimeg giz, dasmer, Iesu ui obapit a kega, Kaka uabi omare. A neis kosker tabakeamlam, a itut abara teter ge, a abi esorgiru.
Iesu uiabi detager, Uaba nole geum kak: ua bakeamlam etomeret kara keimer giz, uiaba ko bakeuare Galilaiaem, uiaba kari erdali.
Ui bakeamlei, dasmer, uader asesered le bakeuare abele uteb, a natomertare gaire zogozogo le giz abele gaire lu uridili ikerare.
A uiaba etami okakis gaire aule, uiaba mer atager, a ko nakuarare gaire mani uiabim abele gaire ares le,
A uiabi kega, Uaba natomertare abara kaimeg giz ki ge tabakeuare, a abi eruam, epe uaba uteid.
Ese opole asoli, a keriba abi idkubi, iaueakai uaba nagri debele.
A uiaba egardarare abele gaire mani, a uiaba ikelare mokakalam uiaba uiabi ereuerem: abele mer esali gaire Iudaia le giz bakedilu peirdi.
Abara kaimeg giz bekeuare Galilaiaem, eleuen gaire le, abele paser ge Iesu uiabi mer tigri.
Uiabi abi erdali, a uiaba abi esorgiru: epe uader le nole oatur kak.
Iesu tabarki, a uiabi detager, kega, Emetu kari nakuar abele sirdam uridili, abele kotor ge pako abele geseb ge.
Dasmer, uaba bakeuare gaire ged narida uridili ko uiabi ereuerem, pako uiabi bapataiso Babe ra nei ge, pako abele Uerem, pako abele Lamar Zogo:
Uaba uiabi ereuerem, a asesered gaire lu uridili kaka uabi detager: dasmer, kaka ko uabi kemem gaire gerger uridili, bakedilu abele geseb ra mop. Amen.
Abele ditimedilu Iesu Keriso ra debe merkem, Ade ra Uerem.
Mokakalam gaire perofeta detali, kega, Kaka emarida karbara merkem mara op, ko paret mara gab;
Le kodo ereretikri soge purge, kega, Paret Iehoua ra gab, barditug abara gab giz.
Ioane ko bapataiso abele soge purge, a marau bapataiso ra obazgeda ko detue adud giz.
Iako abim bakeuare le Iudaia uridili, a uiaba Ierusalemalam, E uiabi bapataiso uridili, abele Ioridano dodo, uiaba detaut uiaba adud giz.
Kamela mus Ioane ra am uali, abara uak kau ra paur; E pem ereg a isas ra sumes are:
E marau, kega, Nerute kara sorge ekas adigir kari tumge, kaka nole abkoreb eparisili a detue abara teter gab mukub.
Kaka uabi bapataiso nilam; E dali uabi bapataiso Lamar Zogolam.
Abele kerker ge, Iesu ekasereder Nazaretalam Galilaiage, Iesu Ioane de bapataiso abele Ioridano ge.
E nilam ekueilu, E egremalu kotor nakesmulu, a Lamar Zogo epereda abi tumge, mokakalam dibadib:
Iako kodo mer uataba kotorlam, kega, Mama kara Uerem nasge, kaka mari sererege.
Dudumge Lamar Zogo abi emarida soge purem.
Foate gaire gerger E soge purge emeri, Satana de abi mirem; abi dog gaire ebur marmar; angela giz abara memeg.
Emetu Ioane didbari, Iesu bakeamulu Galilaiaem, ko marau Ade ra debe merkem, kega,
Kerker ge tabarki, a Ade ra baselaia maike; uaba obazgeda, a debe merkem oituli.
E ekas keper dege Galilaia, E dasmer Simona a Anederea tabara keimer net gurem dikri: abelelam ui darali umele larem.
Iesu ui darali daratager, kega, Kari narmili, kaka uabi depegemelu ko le asaperem.
Ui darali dudum net dekaerei, a abi irmilei.
E ko kebikebi ekasereder, E dasmer Iakobo Zebedaio ra uerem, a Ioane abara keimer, nar ge muigi, a net euelei.
E sobkak ui darali ereretikrei: ui darali Zebedaio uiaba aba dekaerei nar tumge, a gaire memeg, a abi irmilei.
Uiaba Kapernauma tabakeuare; sabath ge E dudum sunago tabao, a ereuerem.
Tabara ereuerem uiaba damered: abelelam E uiabi ereuerem mokakalam le pardale, a nole mokakalam aotale giz.
Nerute le nagri sumes lamar muige abele sunago; E ereretikri, kega,
Iesu Nazaretalam, keriba nako marim? nako, mama tabarki keribi adem dipit? kaka mari opasereret, Ade ra Zogo.
Iesu abi daisumdalu, kega, Bamer, a teosmeda abielam.
Abele sumes lamar abi ezagri, a au ereretikri, epe teosmed abielam.
Uiaba uridili damered, a mer atager, kega, Nalu pedali? nako abele kerkar ereuerem? abelelam sumes lamar giz E sirdam adigir, uiaba abi asoli.
Epe sobkak E ekoseli gaire ged ge Galilaia deraueili.
Uiaba teosmeda sunagolam, sobkak uiaba tabarot kemem Ioane a Iakobo metaem, abele Simona a Anederea ra meta.
Simona kosker ra apu uteid, gem urueri: uiaba sobkak abi etomelu.
E keitekas abi tag erpeilu; sobkak urueri dekaida, E uiabi memeg le.
Kikem, lem baraigida, uiaba abim taraisare gaire, gim le, a gaire le sumes lamar nagri.
Gaire ged uridili netate gedim op meta.
E idigiri gaire tonar gim le, a imuda sumes lamar giz; E nole gaire demoni emarida ko mer egali, abelelam uiaba abi opasereret.
Nede be iuaokaer, E ekueilu a teosmeda, a nogutebem bakeamud, abele esorerapare.
Simona, a abara boai, abi irmilare.
Uiaba abi erdali, uiaba abi detager, kega, Ui uridili mari naraimeli.
E uiabim detaut, kega, Minabakeuare gaire maiged, a kaka marau abele; abelelam kara dorge dali.
E marau muige gaire uiaba sunago Galilaia uridili, a demoni giz imuda.
Abim keitoabuki nerute lepera, a abim ermeder, abi detager, kega, Ese mama laglag, mama umele kari nadgiri.
E abi omare, a tag itrimuda, a abi ituti, a abi detager, kega, Kara lag; ma idigiri
E emetu detager abele mer, sobkak lepera dekaida abielam, E idigir.
E abi mer tigri, a abi emarida,
A abi detager, kega, mamor dasmer, atager kak nerute le; bakeamuda, mabu natomelu abi zogo tarim le, a ikuar gaire lu Mose mer tigri uiabim; atamelam mama emetu idigir.
E bakeamuda, a ditimeda ko daratagerare, a detager deraueili, abelelam Iesu nole umer kak paret kak ekas abele ged, E soge purge emeri; gaire le abim tabakeuare abgedlam.
Gerger giz barki, E iako Kaperenauma uatabu; ui asereda E muige meta.
Sobkak gaire le netate gedim, meta mui osmeda, pako adige; E uiabim Ade ra mer marau.
Uiaba abim tabakeuare, nerute le ibibi egardare, neis a neis le abi bakeuarare.
Uiaba umer kak abi dog maiem bakeuare mitkarlam: uiaba meta tumge ezagarare E muige, a lemlem ismi, uiaba sik dikri gim le tumge igimrare.
Iesu erdarda uiaba oituli, E le ibibi detager, kega, Kara uerem, emetu adem dikri mara uit giz.
Uader aotale giz abele emeri, a tababu dikiapor muige uiaba nerkep ge, kega,
Nalugelam le dali detager mokakalam? E Ade desauersili, nete le umele uit dikri, Ade tepteb?
Sobkak Iesu opasereret muige abara nerkep abele uiaba dikiapor muige uiaba nerkep, E uiabim detager, kega, Nako uaba dikiapor mokakalam muige uaba nerkep?
Nako perper, le ibibi egali, kega, Emetu adem dikri mara uit giz; pako egali, kega, Tekue, mabara sik ekau, a bakeamu?
Ko uabim paret kak, Le la Uerem adigiri gaire uit geseb ge adem dikri, (E le ibibi detager, kega,)
Kaka mari natager, kega, Tekue, mabara sik ekau, a mabara meta bakeamulu.
E ekueda, a sobkak tabara sik ekaida, a E osmeda uiaba op uridili; abelelam uiaba uridili damereda, a Ade despili, kega, Meriba nole dasmerauem tonar mokakalam.
E iako keper dege degemili; gaire le abim tabakeuare, E uiabim ereuerem.
E uteb esaimelu, E Leui, Alefaio ra uerem, dasmer meta dipumeda emeri, E abi detager, kega, Kari narmili, E ekueilu a abi irmili.
Abele iobaru, E abara meta ge emeri leuer ero, telona giz a uit le giz kemem emeri Iesui dog, a abara kaimeg giz; abelelam gaire le uiaba abi irmilare.
Aotale giz a Faresaio giz abi dasmer kemem leuer ero telona giz a uit le giz, uiaba tabara kaimeg giz daratagerare, kega, Nako E kemem leuer ero a ereli telona giz a uit le giz?
Iesu asoli abele mer, E uiabim daratagerare, kega, Saserim le giz lukup kemle lakak, gim le giz lagelag; kaka nole tabarki ko gaire barkak tonar dabgeri, debele gair uit le giz.
Ioane ra kaimeg giz, a gaire Faresaio ra kaimeg giz leuer baili; uiaba tabakeuare a abi detager, kega, Nalugelam Ioane ra kaimeg giz a gaire Faresaio ra kaimeg giz leueru baili, a mara kaimeg giz nole leueru baili?
Iesu uiabi detager, kega, Nako, umele gaire boai le ispida ko leueru baili, le ispida uiabi dog emeri? uiaba umer kak leueru baili, le ispida mena uiabi dog.
Kerker niai tabarki, le ispida uiabielam egared, abele gaire gerger uiaba leueru baili.
Nole le kerkar mog uali itkedi okakis buzibuzi am uali; akeulam buzibuzi mog uali de kerkar mog ualilam ekep itkedi, iako au atoatatoat.
Nole le epaiteret kerkar uaina muige emeret tarpor giz; epe gegur tarpor giz arperiklam, uaina epaiteredlu, epe sor giz adud: mamor ko kerkar gegur tarpor epaiteret kerkar uaina.
Abele iobaru, E ekas kon gedub ge abele sabath; abara kaimeg giz kon itakemarare, a eroarare, gab ge.
Faresaio giz abi detager, kega, Dasmer, nako uiaba lu akerare nole abkoreb sabath?
E uiabi detager, kega, Nako uaba nole etagerare Dauida de ikeli, leuer aro kak, uerer eudili, a gaire abara kaimeg giz?
E Ade zogo meta ge tabalu, Abiatara ra kerker, zogo tarim le, E derser areto eroli, abele nole abkoreb nogle tero, mamor zogozogo le tepteb, E abara kaimeg nakuarare?
E uiabi detager, kega, Sabath emetu ikeli le la uai kedeua, a nole le ikeli sabath uaikedeua;
Abelelam Le la Uerem sabath ra Opole.
E iako sunago balu; abele nerute le tag euselu.
Uiaba abi keikei dasmerare, nako, E abi idigiri sabath ge; uiaba ko abara mer atrumda.
E le tag euselu detager, kega, Eipu ekueda.
E uiabi detager, kega, Nako, abkoreb debe lu ikeli sabath ge, nako adud lu ikeli? ko idigiri, nako ipit eumid? Uiaba bazeguar.
E uiabi urkerem deraueli dasmerare, abara nerkep isir uiaba tonarlam bamesili, E le detager, kega, Mara tag uaimari. Abara tag uaimari; ueakai abara tag ekaida debele mokakalam nerute.
Faresaio giz teosmeda, a sobkak mer atagere, pako Herodiano giz, ko abi ipit eumida.
Iesu a abara kaimeg giz bakeauda abele keper ge; gaire le abi irmili Galilaialam, pako Iudaialam,
Pako Ierusalemalam, pako Idumealam, pako Ioridanolam sager op, pako uiaba maike Turo a Sidona, gaire le abim tabakeuare, abelelam uiaba asereda abara dorge ikeli.
E abara kaimeg giz mer tigri, ko kebi nar tais abi naokaili gaire lelam, uiaba abi atkaplam.
E gaire le nadgirare; abelelam ui uridili gim nagri abi atkap ueakai abi itutilu.
Uite lamar giz abi dasmerare, uiaba abim bakesmeri, a ereretikri, kega, Mamanali Ade ra Uerem.
E uiabim elele mer tigri, uiaba abi atomeret kak.
E paserem ogi, a dabgeri gaire le E laglag; uiaba abim tabakeuare.
E depeger tuelf le, ko abi kemem emri, a E uiabi namarkare ko marau.
Adgiri uiabi nakuarare ko nadgirare gaire gim le, a demoni giz imuda.
E Simona nei atker Peteru;
Pako Iakobo Zebedaio ra uerem, a Ioane Iakobo ra keimer; E uiabi nei atker Boanerege, tonar, Girgir ra uerem:
Pako Anederea, a Filipo, a Batolomaio, a Mataio, a Toma, a Iakobo Alefaia ra uerem, a Tadaio, a Simona Kanana le,
Pako Iuda Isakariota, abi keser keser: uiaba metaem barot.
Ege gaire le netat gedim, abelelam uiaba umer kak leuer aroare.
Abara boai aserare, uiaba tabaos, ko abi terpei; uiaba detager, kega, E paim paim.
Aotale giz Ierusalemalam tabakeuare uiaba detager, kega, Belezebul abi dog, E demoni giz imuda opolelam demoni giz.
E uiabi darabgerare, a uiabi daratagerare gaire mer babisdarie, kega, Nako, Satana umele Satana imuda?
Ese nerute baselaia epuli, abele baselaia umer kak niaiem ekue.
Ese nerute uteb epuli, abele uteb umer kak niaiem ekue.
Ese Satana tababu barili, a epuli, E umer kak niaiem ekue, tabara mop tabarki.
Nerute le umer kak saserim le la meta ge badari, a abara lu itkamri, ese nole kekiam saserim le didbari; iako abara meta itkamri.
Ageakar kak uabi detagereda, kega, Gaire ezubameli, a gaire uit uerem le giz ko detue:
Abele le Lamar Zogo ditagi, nole atue kak niaiem, epe abkoreb abim ikuar niai bodomalam;
Abelelam uiaba detager, kega, Uit lamar abi dog.
Abara keimer pako apu abim tabakeuare; a adige bako, uiaba namarida abi dabgeri.
Gaire le netate gedim abi derumeda bameri; uiaba abi detagerare, kega, Ma dasmer, mara apu a mara keimer giz adige, mari naraimeli.
E uiabi detaut, kega, Nete kara apu a kara keimer giz?
E dasmerare uiaba abi derumeda bameri, E detagereda, kega, Dasmer, kara apu a kara keimer giz!
Abelelam abele le Ade ra lag ikeli, E dali kara keimer, a kara berbet, a kara apu.
E iako degerati ko ereuerem keper tauer ge, gaire le netate gedim abim, abelelam E nar atiem, a emri, uiaba uridili tauer ge bamer.
Gaire mer E uiabim ereuerem mer babisdarie, E uiabidaratagerare abara okadeskeda, kega,
Uaba aserauem; Dasmer, nerute amorda le bakeam ko emor:
E dikri, a uader kep gab dege abi, epe ebur giz kotorlam tabakeuda abele eroare.
Uader kep tumem neidge abi, kebi seb ge; sobkak omeili, abelelam lerkar seb ge:
Gerger eupamada, a eueri, a eumili, abelelam nole sip kak.
Uader kep lu eipu daradara ge omeili, a detarapi, abelelam nole turum kak.
Uader kep debe seb ge abi, a omeili, a esali, a turum turum; a turum therti nagri, a sikesti; a uan handed.
E uiabim detagereda, kega, Le grip nagri ko asoli, debele E asoli.
E tepteb emri, gaire le abi dog emri, pako tuelf le, abi itmer tonar abele mer babisdarie.
E uiabim detagereda, kega, Gaire mu tonar Ade ra baselaia uabi dekuarare ko opaserertem; emetu ikeli abele gaire lu abkoreb uiabim nogle giz:
Abelelam ui ko dasmerare, epe nole asmer kak; a asoli, epe nole asor kak; uiaba depegelam, a uiaba uit ko detue.
E uiabim detagereda, kega, Nako, uaba nole asmer kak abele mer babisdarie? epe nako uaba ko umele gaire mer babisdarie uridili?
Abele amorda le, emor Ade ra mer.
Abele uader le gab ge, abele mer uiabi dog emor; uiaba asereda, epe Satana tabarki, abele mer uiabi nerkep ge emor ekadari.
Abele uader tumem neid ge emor; uiaba abele mer asereda, a sobkak sererge erperida;
Epe nole sip kak muige uiaba nerkep ge, abelelam nole niaiem ekue; menaba asiasi a dedkoli abele merlam tabarki, sobkak uiaba bakesmiri.
Abele uader le eipu daradara ge emor; uiaba abele mer asoli,
Epe gaire dikiapor lu lag geseb ge uiabi nerkep ge badari, pako geseb lu okardarem, pako uader lu lag, abele mer etarapi, epe nole turum kak.
Ege uader emor debe seb ge; uiaba abele mer asoli, a mamor erpeili, a turum turum, uader therti, a uader sikesti, a uader uan handed.
E uiabim detagereda, kega, Nako, lamepa ikedi kumete lokod ge, a laulau lokod ge? epe nole tum ge ikedi lamepa uteb?
Epe nole lu ispili, a nole opasereret kak; pako nole mud ge lu, a nole akmer kak.
Ese nerute le grip nagri ko asoli, debele E asoli.
E uiabim detagereda, kega, Uaba mamoro aserauem; abele tonar uaba detare, ko uabim detare; a ko uabi daisuerare le asereda.
Le nagri, ko abi ikuar; le nole nagri kak, ko ekada abele lu abi dog.
E detagereda, kega, Ade ra baselaia mokakalam le kep dikri seb ge;
E ko uteid, a ekeamlu ki ge a gerger, abele kep uai omeida, a bataile, E nole umer kak nagelam.
Tababu seb ge omeili; uai kekiam, sik keubu, epe turum agiag.
Turum agiag, epe namarida ko tigri, kerker ge nurabi.
E detagereda, kega, Na lu meriba ko abkoreb Ade ra baselaia? na lu abkoreb abele babisdarie?
Abele mokakalam sinapi kep, emetu emor, kebikebi kep tumem gaire kep uridili geseb ge emor,
Emetu emor, E omeida, a aule tumem gaire lu ekekri, epe gaire au tam disiri; a gaire ebur epereda mudi ge igiredi.
E Ade ra mer uiabim detagereda, mokakalam gaire mer babisdarie, abkoreb uiaba umele asoli.
E nole uiabim atager kak, ese nole mer babisdarie; uiaba mud uteb ge, E uiabim, abara kaimeg giz, gaire tonar mer detaut.
Abele gerger kikem, E uiabim daratagereda, kega, Minaba atiem nerut apekem.
Uiaba emetu le lakub emarida, uiaba abi egared nar ge atiem. Uader kebi nar abi doakri.
Au ui tabarki, a gaire zauber nar etatkoi, a mitkar.
E amaz ge kor ge uteidi: uiaba abi itir, a abi detager, kega, Kole, mama laglag ki nabaume?
E tekue, uag daisumda, a gur detager, kega, Bamer, debe meda. Iako uag ekeamulu, ege metalu.
E uiabim daratagereda, kega, Nalugelam uaba geum mokakalam? nako uaba nole oatur kak?
Uiaba au geumu, a mer atagere, kega, Nete dali, uag a gur abi asoli?
Uiaba nerute apek tauer ge tabarki, abele Gadara le la ged.
E narlam eupamada, epe sobkak nerute le uit lamar bada abim obapit: abele le gaire aolam tabakeam,
E gaire ao ge emri; nole le umele abi didbari, a malil par nolea:
Dordor abi didbari, teter ge a tage malil paru, abele tage a teter didbari, E dergeiri; nole le umer kak abi maiem ekepli.
Ki ge, a gerger ge, E mena emerilu abele gaire paser, a gaire ao ge, E ereretikri, a abara gem baker de esakeilu.
E muriz ge Iesui dasmer, E koreder abim a esorgiru.
E au kodo ereretikri, kega, Kaka nako marim, Iesu Ade ra Uerem, au kale? Kaka marim bali Ade ra op, nole kari asiasi nakeli.
Abelelam, E abi detager, kega, Ma lamar uit teosmeda lelam.
E abi itmer, kega, Mara nei nako? E detaut, kega, Kara nei legeona; abelelam keriba gaire.
E elele abim bali, kega, Nole keriba amu kak ab gedelam.
Abele borom au isir gorgor paser ge erueda.
Gaire demoni giz abi damseda, kega, Keribi demarida gaire boromem, ko keriba uiabim badari.
Iesu sobkak uiabi emarida. Abele uit lamar giz teosmeda, a gaire borom ge barti; epe borom isir uamen uamen koreder au gorgorlam keperem, (uiaba maike tu thausan;) iako gune obaiter.
Le giz borom naseserdare koreder ge, a gedim, pako gaire ged daratagerare. Uiaba tabakeuare, a dasmer abele tonar ikeli.
Uiaba Iesuim tabakeuare, uiaba abele le dasmer demoni legeona dedkoli emeri, a ameare, a tonar tonar; epe uiaba geum.
Uiaba le erdali mer poipi detaut gaire tonar le demoni dedkoli, a tonar borom giz.
Uiaba ditimeda abi damosare, ko uiaba ged dekaer.
E nar atiem, le demoni dedkoli abi damos ko abi dog emeri.
E nole laglag, E abi detager, kega, Bakeam mabara ged, a mabara boai, a uiabi natomertauem abele gaire au lu Opole de marim ikeli, a mari omare.
E bakeamud, a ditimeda marau Dekapolem gaire au lu Iesu de abim ikeli; epe uiaba uridili damreda.
Iesu emetu iako atiem nerut apek, gaire le netate gedim abim; E meg tauer ge emeri.
Dasmer, nerute sunago kole tabarki, abara nei Iairo; E abi dasmer, E ekesmiri tabara teter ge,
A abim elele bali, kega, Kara kebi neur maike eumida; debele ma tabakeam a mabara tag abi tum ge dikmerik, ueakai abi idigiri, E ko eded akaida.
E abi kemem bakeam; a gaire le lakub abi irmili, uiaba abi ditkabda.
Abele nerut kosker mam gim tuelf gaire urut babusedari.
E au asias dimegeroa gaire lukup kemlelam, abara lu eseemuda, uiabi nakuarare lukup bodomalam, nole adigir kak, epe mena au gim.
E Iesu ra tonar asoli, E eipu gaire le ekasereder Iesu isorge, abara am uali ekepeli.
Abelelam E detager, kega, Ese kaka abara am uali tepteb ekepeli, kara gim akaida.
Sobkak abara mam diruruarti; E umele abara gem akaida abele gimlam.
Sobkak Iesu abara nerkep ge opasereret nerute adigir osmeda abielam, E gaire le ge eipu egreemalu, a detager, kega, Nete kara am uali ge ekepeli?
Abara kaimeg giz detagereda, kega, Mama dasmer gaire le mari natkabda, nako tonar mama detager, kega, Nete kari dog ekepeli?
E op etarer ko kosker deraimerer abele lu ikeli.
Kosker geum a durdur barki, abelelam E umele abele lu abi dog ikeli, E abara op ge ekesmer, a ageakar abi detager ueeseamur.
E abi detager, kega, Kara neur, mabi oaturlam ma eded akaida; mapodan kem bakeamulu, ma eded akaida mabara gimlam.
E mena detaut abele mer, sunago kole merkem tabarki, a abi detager, kega, Mara neur eumida; nako iako kole bamesili?
Iesu asoli abele mer, E sunago kole detager, kega, Ma nole geum kak epe oituli.
E uiabi daraisumdarda, nole le kak abi irmili, mamor Peteru, a Iakobo, a Ioane Iakobo ra keimer.
Uiaba sunago kole ra meta tabakeuare; a uiabi saserimem nardarare, a ebazoli, ueu baudaredelare.
E badari, a uiabi daratagereda, kega, Nako uaba saserim, a ebazoli? abele neur nole eud kak, E uteidi.
Uiaba abi neg degarare. E emetu uiaba uridili adige namuare, E neur ra aba a apu tegared, a uiaba neis a neis le abi dog, a barot neur ra uteb.
E neur ra tag erpeilu, a abi detager, kega, Talitha kumi; tonar abele mer, Neur, kaka mari natager, Ekue.
Sobkak neur tekuelu, a bakeamulu; tuelf abara urut. Uiaba au kase damreda.
E elele uiabi mer tigri, nole nerute le atomeret kak abele mer; epe E uiabi detager, kega, Debele leuer abi ikuar.
E bakeam ab gedelam, a tabara ged ge tabarki; abara kaimeg giz abi irmili.
Sabath ge, E ditimeda sunago ge ereuerem; gaire le asereda damreda, kega, Nagelam abele gaire dorge abi dog? nako pardali abi ikuar, ueakai gaire dorge adigir mokakalam abara tag ikeli?
Nako nole tonar le abele? nako nole Maria rauerem, Iakobo ra keimer, a Iose, a Iuda, a Simona? nako abara berbet nole meribi dog? uiaba abi derar.
Iesu uiabi daratagereda, kega, Nole perofeta ekekri, tepteb abara ged ge, a abara boai, a abara uteb ge.
E nole umer kak nerut adigir ikeli peike, abele dorge tepteb, abara tag gaire gim le dikmerik, a uiabi nadgirauem.
E au damreda uiabielam uatur kak. E bakeamuda deraueida abele gaire kebi uteb ge, a okadeskeda.
E tuelf le darabgerare, a ditimeda uiabi namarida neisi le a neisi le; a adigir uiabi nakuarare tumem gaire uite lamar;
E uiabi mer tigri, kega, Lu aisis kak abele bakeam, no koket tepteb; nolo epei kak, nole leuer kak, a nole mani kak muige uak;
A no teter gab ameare; a nole neis am uali ameare.
E uiabi daratagereda, kega, Uaba nerute meta ge badari, emri abele, a iako bakeauare.
Uiaba le giz uabi agared kak, a nole uabi asor kak, uaba bakeam abele gedelam, sep ditkeda uaba teter gablam uiabi atamelam. Ageakar, kaka uabi detagereda, kega, Niaiem gerger itmer, kebi bodamalam Sodomaem a Gomoraem tumem abele ged ge.
Uiaba bakeauda, a marau, kega, Mamor uaba gaire le obazegeda.
Gaire uit lamar uiaba namuda, a gaire gim le uiaba ide epaitered, a uiabi nadgirare.
Heroda opole asoli, abelelam abara nei ekoseli; E detager, kega, Ioane Bapataiso eded akaida eudelam, abelelam E gaire adigir ikeli.
Uader detager, kega, Elia pedali. Uader detager, kega, Perofeta pedali, abelelam E nerute perofeta mokakalam.
Heroda asoli, E detager, kega, Ioane pedali, karielam abara kerem derapeida, E eded akaida eudelam.
Emetu Heroda namarkare Ioane terpeirare, a abi didbare muige au dubare meta ge Herodialam, Filipo ra kosker abara narbet: abelelam E abi ispilu.
Abelelam Ioane Heroda detager, kega, Nole marim abkoreb mara narbet ra kosker ispida.
Abelelam Herodia Ioane urker, a E lagelag abi ipit; a nole umer kak;
Abelelam Heroda Ioane geum, E opasereret Ioane barkak tonar, a zogo le, E abi asesereda. E abi asoli, a ikeli gaire dorge, a abi sererge asoli.
Gerger abkoreb tabarki, abele gerger Heroda eosmelu, E dersemer uiabim gaire opole giz, a gaire kole, a gaire tarim le Galilaia ge;
Herodia ra neur balu, a ginar diger, Heroda pako uiaba abi dog emri a sererge; opole neur detager, kega, Kari nautumer lu mara laglag, kaka mari nakuar.
E abi mer nakesmulu detager, kega, Kaka mari nakuar gaire lu mama kari nautumer, mokakalam kara baselaia mog.
E teosmeda, a abara apu detager, kega, Nalu kaka damos? Abara apu detager, kega, Ioane Bapataiso ra kerem.
Sobkak E iako opole badari, a abi detager, kega, Kaka laglag mama mena kari nakuar Ioane Bapataiso ra kerem abele tanelu ge.
Opole ra nerkep beber barki; epe E nole abi azer kak, abele mer akesmulam, a uiabielam abi dog bamer leuer eroare.
Opole sobkak memeg le namarida, a abi mer tigri, kega, Abara kerem tegaret.
E bakeamuda, a Ioane ra kerem derapeida muige au dubare meta ge, a abara kerem tegaret tanelu ge, a neur ikuar; a neur abara apu ikuar.
Ioane ra kaimeg giz aserare, ui bakeuare, a abara gem tegardare, a ao ge ikedarare.
Iesu ra kaimeg giz tabakeuare abim; a abim daratagerare gaire dorge uiaba ikelare, a uiaba ereuerem.
E uiabi detagereda, kega, Mi nabakeuare le kak utebem, ueakai ner nabazier. Abelelam gaire le uatupili, a nole uteb ko leuer ero.
Uiaba nar ge gumik atiem abele le kak utebem.
Gaire le lakub dasmer uiaba atiem, gaire le abi opaserertem, a koreder ge abim gaire gedelam uridili, uiaba kekiam tabarki, a netat gedim abim.
E bakeam a gaire le dasmerauem, a uiabi nasge, abelelam uiaba mokakalam mamoe giz nole le asesered kak; a E uiabi ditimeda ereuerem gaire lu dordor.
Kikem, abara kaimeg giz abim tabakeuare, a detager, kega, Soge pur ike, a kikem:
Uiabi namarkare gaire gedim, a gaire utebem, leuer arapem uiaba aroem; abelelam uiaba nole leuer kak.
E uiabi detagereda, kega, Uaba uiabi leuer nakuarare. Uiaba abi detager, kega, Nako, keriba bakeuare leuer arapem tu handed denari ko bodomalam, ko uiabi asisiem?
E uiabi detagereda, kega, Naket areto uabi dog? bakeam dasmer. Uiaba edali, a detager, kega, Faif, a neis lar.
E uiabi mer tigri ko nosik bameri tumem abele golegole soge ge.
Uiaba nosik bameri, uader uan handed nosik, uader fifeti nosik.
E emetu faif areto tais, a neisi lar, E kotor dimiruarti, a esoao, a areto itur; a abara kaimeg giz nakuarare uiaba opem idedi; E neisi lar ditker uiabim uridili.
Uiaba uridili leuer eroare, a kem osmeda.
Uiaba leuer mog, a lar mog etakarare, epe tuelf epei osmeda.
Mokakalam faif thausan gaire kimiar, areto eroare.
E sobkak abara kaimeg giz elele daratirieda nar ge bartiri, ko atiem nerut apekem Bethesaida opem, abara dorge gaire le namarida.
E emetu uiabi namarida, E paserem ogi esorerapare.
Bakedilu abele kikem, nar eip karem ge, a Iesu tepteb geseb ge emrilu.
E uiabi darasmerare uzelam sagim, abelelam uag opem uami; ki apek foa, E uiabim tabarki, zauber tum ge ekas; mokakalam E uiaba dege ekas.
Uiaba abi erdali zauber tum ge ekas, uiaba dikiapor lamar pedali, epe uiaba au ereretikri;
Abelelam ui uridili abi dasmer, epe uiaba geum. Sobkak E uiabi detagereda, kega, Saserimem; kai nali, nole geum kak.
E uiabim nar ge ekauererti; epe uag ekaida: uiaba abi au kase damereda.
Uiaba nole akiapor kak abele areto, abelelam uiaba nerkep kelarkelar.
Uiaba emetu esaimeda atiem, uiaba tabarki Genesareta ged, a ged ge ekarida.
Uiaba emetu ekarida narlam, sobkak uiabi abi opasereretem,
A gedim kored deraueida, a ditimeda gim le giz bakuarda tumem sik, a kei tegardare abele uteb Iesu emri.
Abele uteb, a ged, a gedub E tabarki, uiaba gaire gim le tegardare ugab ge ikedi, a abi damsare ko abara am uali dege ekpi; uiaba uridili abi ekpi nadgirauem.
Faresaio giz, a uader aotale giz, netat gedim abim Ierusalemalam.
Uiaba dasmer uader abara kaimeg giz areto er oare a ogog tag arub kak, uiaba mer mer.
Abelelam Faresaio giz, a Iudaia giz, nole leuer aro kak, ese nole mamoro tag ogarub kak, uiaba aule ra tonar irmirauem.
Uiaba tabarki leuer araplam, nole leuer aro kak, ese nole ogarup kak. A dordor tonar uiaba erpei, a ikerare, tanelu ogdirup, a tanelu tonar, a malil tanelu, a gaire sik.
Faresaio giz a aotale giz abi itmer, kega, Nako mara kaimeg giz nole irmili aule giz ra tonar, epe leuer arouem a tag ogarup kak?
E uiabi daratagereda, kega, Isaia mamoro uabim bes le giz perofetaem, emetu detali, kega, Abele ged ge kari naospereda uiaba mitelam, a uiaba nerkep kara muriz ge.
Uiaba sagim karim esorerapare, a gaire le la tonar ereuerem lelam.
Uaba Ade ra gelar dekaierta, a le la tonar elele erpei.
E uiabi daratagereda, kega, Uaba tonar Ade ra gelar dituaki, ueakai uaba tonar irmireda.
Mose detager, kega, Mabi abera, a mabi apuera naospili; E dali tabara aba a apu desauersili, debele abi ipit eumilu:
Epe uaba detagerare, kega, Ese nerute le tabara aba, a apu detager, kega, Abele kara lu mari upinati Korabana, tonar abele, Emetu Adim ikuar;
Uaba nole abi amari kak, ko nerut lu ikeli abem a apuem;
Abele uaba tonar lelam, Ade ra mer dedkoli; a gaire lu mokakalam uaba ikeli.
Ege E iako gaire le lakub derabgerare abim, E uiabi detagereda, kega, Uaba uridili kari asoli pako akmerem:
Nole sor lu le nerkep ge badari, umele abi dedkoli; mamoro gaire lu abi nerkeplam osmeda, abele gaire lu le dedkoli.
Ese nerute le grip nagri ko asoli, debele E asoli.
E metaem balu gaire le kublam, abara kaimeg giz abim eutumer tonar mer babisdarie.
E uiabim daratagereda, kega, Nako uaba ko nole umer kak? Nako uaba nole akmer kak, nole sor lu le kem ge badari, umele le dedkoli;
Abelelam nole abara kem ge badari, mamor teibur ge, a sumez ge imuda, a leuer uridili mamor ikeroa?
Edetager, kega, Abele lu lelam osmeda, abele lu le dedkoli.
Abelelam mui le nerkeplam osmeda gaire adud dikiapor, a kogem, a eruam, a le ipit eumilu, a keserkeser,
A lu lag, a uit tonar, a okardar, a opelid, a erkepagau, a ezu bameli, a baospili, a paim tonar:
Abele gaire adud tonar pedali mui nerkeplam eosmeda, a le dedkoli.
E tekue ab gedelam, a nener Turo a Sidona bakeamulu. E nerute meta badari, a nole lakak nerute le abi dasmer; epe E nole umer kak ispili.
Nerute kosker, abara neur nagri uit lamar, E asoli Iesu pedali, E tabakeam a Iesu ra teter ge asorgiru:
Abele kosker Heleni kosker, Surofoiniki osmeda. E Iesui damos ko demoni imuda abara neurlam.
Epe E abi detager, kega, Kekiam gaire uerem kem osmeda; nole abkoreb uerem ra leuer tais, a omai giz nakuarare.
Kosker abi detaut, kega, Ageakar, Opole; epe omai giz deroli laulau muige gaire leuer puipi uerem giz aroem.
E koskerim detager, kega, Abele merlam, ma bakeam; demoni emetu bakeam marara neurlam.
Kosker tabara meta tabarki, E dasmer demoni nole akar, a abara neur uteidilu.
E iako bakeamulu Turo a Sidona nenerlam, a Galilaia keper tabarki, eipu Dekapoli.
Uiaba abim tegared nerut lo grip batapeli, a lukluk mer; uiaba abi damos ko tabara tag abi tum ge dikmerik.
E gumik abi tegared gaire lekublam, a abara neisi baur kei abara neis grip deraimilu, a mosu itu, a abara uerut itutilu;
A kotorem egremalu, a ner batauerdelu, a abi detager, kega, Efatha, tonar abele mer, Diski.
Sobkak abara neis grip darauskilu, a abara uerut kerar detue, a E barkak mer egali.
E uiabim mer tigri, kega, Nole, nerute le atager kak: E sagim uiabim mer tigri, uiaba elele daratagerare abele lu.
Uiaba au kase damereda, kega, E mamoro ikeroa gaire lu uridili: E gaire grip batapeli ikeli a asoli, a gaire te dabim, ko mer detaut.
Abele gaire gerger, dordor le lakub, a uiaba nole leuer kak, E tabara kaimeg giz darabgerare, a uiabi detagereda, kega,
Kaka le lakub nasenase, abelelam uiaba thri gerger kari dog emri, a nole leuer aro kak;
Ese kaka uiabi meta namarida, a nole leuer aro kak, uiaba gab ge durdur; abelelam uader muriz gedelam.
Abara kaimeg giz abi detagerare, kega, Nagelam areto, abele soge purge, uiabi darasisieda?
E uiabim nautumereda, kega, Nako, naket areto uabi dog? Uiaba detagerare, kega, Sefen.
E le lakub mer tigri ko seb ge emereda; E gaire areto sefen tekadarare, a esoao, a itiri, a abara kaimeg giz nakuarare, uiaba opem ikedi; a uiaba le lakub opem ikedi.
Uader kebi lar uiabi dog: Iesu esoao, a uiabi detagereda ko ikedi.
Uiaba eroare, a kem osmeda: a uiaba leuer mogmog etaker, a gaire epei sefen arot.
Maike foa thausan, ui uridili leuer eroare; E uiabi namarida.
Sobkak E, pako abara kaimeg giz, nar ge ekauererti, a ged Dalmanutha atiem.
Faresaio giz abim tabakeuare, a ditimeda abi basaret, ko abi mirem, abi itmer atamelam kotorlam.
E au nerezi muige abara mar, kega, Nako abele nosik le atamelam deraimer? Ageakar, kak uabi detagereda, kega, Nole akuar kak atamelam abele nosik le.
E uiabi dekaer, iako nar ge ekauererti, a nerut apek atiem.
Uiaba okataprik ko leuer ais; no netat areto uiabi dog nar ge.
E uiabi mer tigri, kega, Beber dasmer, abele Faresaio ra leuen, a Heroda ra leuen mamoro dasmer.
Uiaba mer atagere, kega, Abelelam meriba nole areto kak.
Epe Iesu opasereret, E uiabi detager, kega, Nako uaba mer atager abele nole leuer kak? Nako uaba nole umer kak, uaba nole akiapor kak? nako uaba tumtum nerkep?
Nako uaba pone nagri, a nole asmer kak? a grip nagri, a nole asor kak? a nole akiapor kak?
Ababurge kaka faif areto itiri uiabim faif thausan, naket epei osmeda uaba etaker abele leuer mog? Uiaba abi detager, kega, Tuelf.
A gaire areto sefen uiabi foa thausan, naket epei osmeda uaba etaker abele leuer mog? Uiaba abi detager, kega, Sefen.
E uiabi daratagereda, kega, Nako uaba nole akiapor kak?
Uiaba Bethesaida tabakeuare. Uiaba nerute le asamasam abim tegaret, a abi damos ko abi itut.
E tage asamasam le erpei, a abi dadkimortare abgedelam; E emetu abara neis pone mos ermeda, a tage abi tumge ikedi, E abi itmer, kega, Nako ma nole nerute lu dasmer?
E kotor dasmer, a detager, kega, Kaka gaire le dasmer, mokakalam dordor lu nakasir.
E iako tabara tage ikedi tumem abara neis pone; a E lidem dasmer, E ueakai debele, a gaire lu mamoro dasmer.
E abi namarida abara metaem, a detager, kega, Nole bakeamu utebem abele.
Iesu pako, abara kaimeg giz, gaire utebem Kaisaria Filipo bakeuare; eipu gab ge, Iesu abara kaimeg giz eutumer, kega, Nako gaire le natagere, kaka nete?
Uiaba detaut, kega, Ioane Bapataiso; epe uader detager, Elia; a uader detager, Nerute perofeta giz.
E uiabi daratagereda, kega, Nako uaba detager, kaka nete? Peteru abi detaut, kega, Mama Keriso.
E uiabi mer tigri, nole nerut le abi atager kak abele.
E ditimeda uiabi ereuerem, Le la Uerem ko asiasi, a aule giz abi derar, a gaire tarim le, a zogozogo le giz, a aotale giz, ko abi ipit eumilu, a keubu thri gerger E iako eded akaida.
E paret kak detager abele mer. Ege Peteru abi datkimalu, a ditimeda abi daisumda.
