Iesu emetu detaut abele gaire mer, E pako abara kaimeg giz bakeuare dodo datuparare, nei Kederon, E pako abara kaimeg giz abele gedubem tabarki.
Iuda, abi keserkeser, umele abele uteb: abelelam Iesu gaire bakeam abele uteb, kemem abara kaimeg giz.
Iuda taraisare gaire ares le, a gaire tarim le, uiabielam gaire zogo le, a gaire Faresaio, a kei tabarkare gaire lamepa kem, a gaire be kem, a gaire ares lu.
Iesu umele gaire lu ko abim tabarki, E maiem bakeamulu, a uiabim detager, kega, Netede uaba deraimerare?
Uiaba abi detaut, kega, Iesu Nazaret le. Iesu uiabim detaut, kega, Kai nali. Iuda, abi keserkeser, uiabi kemem bako.
Emetu Iesu detager, kega, Kai nali, uiaba bazik bakeuare, a seb ge bakesmer.
E iako uiabim eutumer, kega, Netede uaba deraimerare? Uiaba detaut, kega, Iesu Nazaret le.
Iesu detaut, kega, Kaka emetu uabi detagereda, kega, Kai nali: ese uaba kari naraimeli, uiabi namarkare, ko bakeuare:
Ueakai bakedida abara mer, kega, Nole nerute le abi uiabielam mama kari nakuar.
Simona Peteru nagri tebur ausos tulik, E iselu, a etaueriklu tarim zogozogo le ra memeg le, a abara tuter laip dikiam. Nei abele memeg Maliko.
Iesu Peteru detager, kega, Mabara tebur ausos tulik iako sorge dasiri: nako, kaka nole are kak abele tanelu Baba de kari nakuar?
Kole ra ares le giz, a Iudaia tarim le, Iesu terpeirare, a abi didbarare.
Kekiam uiaba abi tegaret Anaem; abelelam E Kaiafa ra naiuet, tarim zogo le abele urut ge.
Abele Kaiafa Iudaia giz daratagerare, kega, Debele netate le ko eumilu ab ged ra kes.
Simona Peteru, a nerute kaimeg giz abi irmilei: tarim zogozogo le opasereret abele nerute kaimeg giz, E Iesu dog balu tarim zogo le ra meta ge;
Peteru meta te ge tekueilu. Abele nerute kaimeg giz tarim zogo le opasereret, iako teosmelu, a neur te asesered detaut, a Peteru muige tegaredilu.
Neur te asesered Peteruim detager, kega, Nako, ma nole nerute abara kaimeg giz? E detaut, kega, Kaka nole.
Gaire memeg le a gaire kole bako, a ur etoamerdare zirulam; a uiaba gebaugare: Peteru ui kemem, bako gebaugare.
Tarim zogo le Iesu eutumer uiabielam abara kaimeg giz, pako ereuer tonar.
Iesu abi detaut, kega, Kaka paret kak gesepem detaut; kaka sunago ge ereuerem, a zogo meta ge, Iudaia giz netate uteb ge; kaka nole nerute lu mude ge detaut.
Nalugem ma kari nautumer? uiabi nautumerare, gaire le kara mer aserare, kaka uiabi detagereda: dasmer, uiaba umele gaire mer kaka detaut.
E emetu abele ge detaut, nerute tarim le abele tekueilu Iesu tagu detapi, a detager kega, Nako, ma detaut mokakalam zogo kemleem?
Iesu abi detaut, kega, Ese kaka adud mer detaut, detomerti nalu adud: ese debe mer, nalugelam ma kari napit?
Ana abi didbari a emarida Kaiafaem, zogo tarim le.
Simona Peteru ekueilu ge bauger. Uiaba abi detager, kega, Nako, ma nole nerute abara kaimeg giz? E asared, a detaut, kega, Kaka nole.
Nerute zogo tarim le la memeg le, boai abele le Peteru abara laip dismilu, detaut, kega, Nako, kaka nole mari nasmer abi dog gedub ge?
Peteru iako asared: epe sobkak kimiar faul ereretikri.
Uiaba Iesu Kaiafaelam tagaret kot metaem, abele banege. Uiaba nole barot abele kot meta, ueakai uiaba nole uit kak, ko paseka eroli.
Pilato uiabim eosmeda, a detager, kega, Nako uaba mer ko aisare le idali?
Uiaba abi detaut, kega, Ese E nole adud ikeli, keriba nole abi emarik marim.
Pilato uiabim detaut, kega, Uaba abi egardare, a abi eutumer abkoreb uaba gelar. Iudaia giz abi detaut, kega, Nole keribim abkoreb ko le ipit eumida:
Ueakai Iesu ra mer bakedida, E emetu detager, a natomertare tonar eud E ko eumilu.
Pilato iako balu kot metaem, a Iesu dabgeri, a abi detager, kega, Nako, ma Iudaia giz ra Opole?
Iesu detaut, kega, Nako, mabu detager abele, ege nerute le mari natageri?
Pilato detaut, kega, Nako, kaka Iudaia le? Mara ged, a zogo tarim le giz mari namarida karim: nalu ma ikeli?
Iesu detaut, kega, Kara baselaia nole geseplam: ese kara baselaia geseplam, gaire kara kaimeg giz ko bares, ueakai nole kari emarik gaire Iudaiaem: peirdi, kara baselaia nole abele ge lam.
Pilato abi detager, kega, Nako, ma opole? Iesu detaut, kega, Ma detager kaka opole. Abelelam kaka naosmeda, abelelam kaka gesepem tarabu, ueakai kaka ko ageakar ageakarem. Gaire le uridili ageakalam kara kodo mer asoli.
Pilato de abi detaut, kega, Nalu ageakar? Emetu abele detager, E iako osmeda uiabim gaire Iudaia le, a uiabim detager, kega, Kaka nole uit ardar kak abi dog.
Epe uaba tonar ka ko uabim amariklu nerute le paseka kerker ge: nako, uaba lagelag ka ko uabim emarida Iudaia giz Opole?
Uiaba iako au ereretikri, a detager, kega, Nole E dali, debele Barabasa. Ege Barabasa nerute eruam le.
Pilato Iesu tegaret, a abi damrik.
Gaire ares le zegerzeger aper euerare, a abi kerem ge ameare, a abi dameare mam mam am uali;
A abim tabarki, a detaut, kega, Uaiai, Iudaia giz Opole! Uiaba abi detapiare.
Pilato iako teosmelu, a uiabi detager, kega, Dasmer, kaka abi tegaret uabim, ueakai uaba dasmer kaka nole nerute uit ardar kak abi dog.
Iesu teosmeda, zegerzeger aper dameare, a mam mam am uali dameare. Pilato uiabi detager, kega, Le das!
Gaire zogo tarim le, a gaire asesered le abi dasmer, uiaba elele ereretikri, kega, Satauroem, satauroem. Pilato uiabim detaut, kega, Ua abi egardare, a satauroem: abelelam kaka nole nerute uit ardar kak abi dog.
Gaire Iudaia le abi detaut, kega, Keriba gelar nagri, abkoreb abele gelar E ko eumida, abelelam tababu akailu Ade ra Uerem.
Pilato abele mer asoli, E au geum;
E iako kot meta balu, a Iesuim eutumer, kega, Ma na gedelam? Iesu nole abim etkalu.
Pilato abi detager, kega, Nako, ma nole karim natkarti? ma nole umele kara nagri adigir ko mari satauroem, a kara nagri adigir ko mari emariklu?
Iesu detaut, kega, Ese nole mari nakuar kotorlam, Ma nole adigir nagri kari tumge: abelelam au uit abele le kari nakuar marim.
Abele ge lam Pilato deraimer ko abi emariklu: Iudaia giz elele ereretikri, kega, Ese ma abele le emarida, ma nole Kaisara ra boai: abele le tababu akailu opole, E Kaisara ra keubu le.
Pilato abele mer asoli, E Iesu adige tegaret, a kot bau ge emerilu, nei atker, Baker esegemelu, a Heberu kodo mer, Gabatha.
Kerker ge Paseka derser: mokakalam eipu gerger. E Iudaia giz detager, kega, Dasmer, uaba Opole!
Uiaba elele ereretikri, kega, Egardare, egardare, abi satauroem. Pilato uiabi detager, kega, Nako, kaka uaba Opole satauroem? Gaire zogo tarim le etkalu, kega, Keriba nole opole kak, Kaisara tepteb.
E abi emarik uiabim, ko satauroem.
Uiaba Iesu egardare: E osmeda tabara satauro tababu kodorom, a utebem bakeam, nei atker, Kerem lid ra uteb, Heberu nei, Gologotha:
Abele uteb ge, uiaba abi satauroem, neisi le abi kemem, nerute apek, a nerute apek, a Iesu eipu.
Pilato atamelam jauali detali, a tumem satauro dikmerik. Abele detali kega, IESU NAZARETA LE, IUDAIA LE GIZ RA OPOLE.
Dordor Iudaia giz abele jauali detagerare: abelelam maike au uteb abele uteb uiaba Iesu satauroem: emetu detali Heberu, a Helene, a Roma ra kodo mer.
Iudaia zogo tarim le Pilatoim detaut, kega, Nole autar kak, Iudaia giz Opole; epe tababu detager, kega, Kaka Iudaia giz Opole.
Pilato detaut, kega, Abele kaka detali, kaka detali.
Gaire ares le emetu Iesu satauroem, uiaba abara am uali ekadarare, a foa derapeir, abkoreb uiaba ares le; am uali kot ko: abele am uali kot nole adket kak, kemer kemer euer.
Uiaba mer atagere, kega, Meriba nole aspas kak, a debele lugulug deraimer niti ra lu: ueakai jauali bakedida, kega, Uiaba kara am uali derapeiare, a kara am uali kot lugulug ikeli. Abele gaire lu ares le giz ikeli.
Iesu ra satauro dege abara apu ekueilu, pako abara apu ra keimer, Maria, Kelopa ra kosker, a Maria Magadalena.
Iesu abara apu dasmer, pako abele kaimeg E nasge, maike tekueilu, E abara apu detager, kega, Kosker, dasmer mara uerem!
E ko detager abele kaimeg, Dasmer mara apu! Abele kaimeg abi tegaredelu abara uteb abele haua ge.
Abele iobaru, Iesu umele, kega, Gaire lu uridili eseemuda. Ueakai jauali bakedida, E detager, kega, Kaka ni ap.
Abele ge nerute tanelu, mitkar uinega: uiaba sab akmei uinega de, a hisop paikai ge dikmeriklu, a abara te ge agisilu.
Emetu Iesu uinega erpeilu, E detager, kega, Eseemuda: E abara kerem esorgiru, a lamar emariklu.
Iudaia giz Pilatoim bareda ko uiaba teter erapei, a uiaba egardare, ueakai uiaba gem nole emerered sabath ge, (abelelam gerger derser, au gerger abele sabath.)
Uiaba gaire ares le tabakeuare, a kekiam le ra teter erapei, a nerute abi kemem satauro:
Epe uiaba Iesuim tabarki, a dasmer E eumida, uiaba nole abara teter arapeir kak:
Epe nerute uiaba gaire ares le abi ber ge dabu ekos, a sobkak mam a ni babuser.
Le ardali ageakarem, abara mer ageakar: E umele, ageakar E detaut, ueakai uaba oituli.
Emetu ikeli abele gaire lu, ueakai bakedida abele mer detali, kega, Nole arapeir kak nerute abara lid.
Nerute mer emetu detali, kega, Uiaba ko abi dasmer uiaba dab akoselam.
Abele iobaru, Iosefa Arimathea le, nerute Iesu ra kaimeg, E gumik abelelam E Iudaia giz geum, a Pilatoi damos ko Iesu ra gem tegaret: ege Pilato emarik. E tabakeam, a Iesu ra gem egaret.
Nikodemo ko tabakeam, abele le ki ge Iesuim bakeam, E muro tais a alo atapetem, mokakalam uan handed paun beber.
Uiaba Iesu ra gem egardare a uali lino de sopem, kemem gaire debe lagelag lu, mokakalam Iudaia giz ra tonar etkobei.
Abele gedub ge, uteb uiaba Iesu satauroem, nagri kerkar ao, nole eud le akedir kak.
Uiaba Iesu abele ge ikedilu, abelelam gerger ge derser uiaba Iudaia le, (epe ao maike.)
Kekiam gerger sefen, Maria Magadalena tabakeam, bane ge, aoem, a baker dasmer, emetu adem aolam.
E koreder emerilu, a Simona Peteruim tabarki, pako nerute memeg le Iesu nasge, a uiabi daratager, kega, Uiaba emetu Opole egaret aolam, keriba umer kak nade uiaba abi ikedi.
Peteru, pako abele nerute kaimeg osmelei, a bakeamulei aoem.
Ui koreder emerilei: nerute kaimeg Peteru esaimeda, a ao ge kekiam tabarki;
E diketilu, a uali dasmer ipe; E nole bao.
Simona Peteru ko tabarki, abi irmili, a ao ge balu; a uali lino dasmer ipe,
Pako mog uali abara kerem sopem, nole netate ipe kemem uali lino, tepteb ipe nerute uteb nole atarat kak.
Nerute kaimeg balu ko, abele le kekiam aoem tabarki, E ko dasmer, a oituli.
Uiaba nole akmer kak abele mer detali, kega, Abkoreb abim iako eded akaida eudelam.
Neisi kaimeg iako tabara uteb bakeamudariei.
Maria tekue adige ao ge ezoli: E tegreamalu a ezoli, a dasmer muige abele ao ge;
E neisi angela darasmer, zazer uali darame eder emrilei, nerute kerem ge, a nerute teter ge, abele uteb Iesu ra gem ikedilu.
Uiaba abi detager, kega, Kosker, nalugem mama ezoli? E uiabim detaut, kega, Abelelam uiaba kara Opole egareda, kaka umer kak abele uteb uiaba abi ikedarare.
Emetu abele detager, E egreamalu, a Iesu dasmer tekue, E nole umer kak Iesu pedali.
Iesu abi detaut, kega, Kosker, nalugem ma ezoli? ma niti deraimeri? E dikiapor E gedub paret arup le, E abi detaut, kega, Kole, ese mama abi egaret, kari natager abele uteb mama abi ikedi, ueakai kaka ko abi agaretelu.
Iesu abi detager, kega, Maria. E tegreamalu a abi detager, kega, Raboni: tonar, Ereue le.
Iesu abi detaut, kega, Nole kari atutir kak; abelelam kaka nole karba Babim ogi: bakeamulu uiabim kara keimer giz, a uiabi daratagerare, kega, Kaka Abem pako uaba Aba ogi, kara Ade a uaba Ade.
Maria Magadalena kei bakeamulu, a kaimeg giz daratagerare, kega, Kaka emetu Opole dasmer; pako tonar E emetu detager abele abim.
Ki ge abele gerger, kekiam gaire sefen, emetu demare gaire te abele uteb uiaba netate gedim, abelelam uiaba Iudaia le geum ge, Iesu tabakeamulu a eipu ekueilu, a uiabi detager, kega, Mapodan uabim.
Emetu abele detager, E abara neisi tag a abara ber uiabi natomelu. Abara kaimeg giz sererge Opole dasmer.
Iesu iako uiabi detager, kega, Mapodon uabim: kaka uabi namarida mokakalam Baba kare namarida.
E emetu abele detager, E uiabim nerezi, a detager, kega, Lamar Zogo egaret:
Abele gaire le la uit uaba ko emarik, abele ko uiabim emarik: abele uaba dekaer, abele ko dekaer.
Toma, nerute tuelf lelam, nei atker Didumo, nole uiabi dog kerker Iesu tabarki.
Kaimeg giz abi detager, kega, Keriba emetu Opole dasmer. E uiabim detaut, kega, Ese kaka nole dasmer sok tulik ziz abara neisi tag, a kara baur kei sok tulik ziz ge aziriklu, a kara tag abara ber ge aziriklu, kaka nole uatur kak.
Gaire gerger eit iobaru, abara kaimeg giz muige meta, a Toma uiabim kemem. Gaire te emetu demare, Iesu batimedilu, a uiabim eipu ekueilu, a detager, kega, Mapodan uabim.
E Toma detager, kega, Mabara baur kei tekau, a dasmer kara neisi tag; a mabara tag tekau, a kara ber ge aziriklu: ma nole uatur kak, debele oituli.
Toma abi detaut, kega, Kara Opole, a kara Ade.
Iesu abi detaut, kega, Toma ma oituli abelelam ma kari dasmer: uiaba uerkab le gaire le oituli, a nole asmer kak.
Dordor atamelam Iesu ikelare opem abara kaimeg giz, a nole detali abele jauali ge:
Emetu abele gaire lu detali ueakai uaba dikiaporauem, kega, Iesu Keriso kar, Ade ra Uerem: ueakai uaba onatereda, uaba ko eded nagri abi neilam.
Abele lu iobaru, Iesu iako tababu natomertare uiabim kaimeg giz, Tiberia keper ge; abele tonar tabara natomertare.
Netate gedim Simona Peteru, a Toma, nei atker Didumo, a Nathaniela, Kana Galilaia le, a neisi Zebedaio ra uerem, a neisi abara kaimeg giz.
Simona Peteru uiabi detager, kega, Kai nabakeamulu net asaperem. Uiaba abi detaut, kega, Ki ko nabakeuare mari kemem. Uiaba bakeuare, a nar ge ekauererti; abele ki ge, uiaba nole lar kak.
Ege idim ge, Iesu tauer ge tekueilu: kaimeg giz nole umer kak Iesu dali.
Iesu uiabi detager, Kega, Omasker, nako, uaba leuer nagri? Uiaba abi detaut, kega, Nolea.
E uiabim detager, kega, Net dikri nar tuter peik, a uaba ko dasmer. Uiaba dikri, epe uiaba umer kak net eguatumur, abelelam lar dordor.
Abele kaimeg Iesu nasge Peteru detager, kega, Opole pedali. Simona Peteru asoli, kega, Opole pedali, E tabara uali kot ame (abelelam E no gem), E gurim eupamalu.
Kaier kaimeg giz tabakeuare kebi nar tumge (abelelam uiaba nole muriz geseplam, mokakalam fifte eit fathom), net eguatumur gaire lar kem.
Uiaba gesepem tabarki, uiaba ur dasmer, a lar tumge, pako leuer.
Iesu uiabi detager, kega, Uader lar kei tais uaba asaperem peirdi.
Simona Peteru ekauerelu, a net gesepem eguatumulu, mitkar au larlam, uan handed a fifte thri: a net nole atoat kak au larlam.
Iesu uiabi detager, kega, Tabakeuare, leuer aroare. Nole nerute uiabielam kaimeg giz saserimem abim eutumer, kega, Ma nete? abelelam uiaba umele Opole dali.
Iesu tabakeamulu leuer ais, a uiabi ikuar pako lar kem.
Abele thri Iesu tababu natomertare uiabim kaimeg giz, keubu E eded akaida eudelam.
Uiaba emetu eroare, Iesu Simona Peteru detager, kega, Simona, Iona ra uerem, ma kari lag uiabi tumge? E abi detager, kega, Eko, Opole; ma umele kaka mari lag. E abi detager, kega, Kara kebi mamoe giz darasisiare.
E iako neisi abi detager, kega, Simona, Iona ra uerem, ma kari lag? E abi detager, kega, Eko, Opole; ma umele kaka mari lag. E abi detager, kega, Kara mamoe giz darasisiare.
E iako thri abi detager, kega, Simona, Iona ra uerem, ma kari lag? Peteru okabatageli abelelam E thri abi detager, kega, Ma kari lag? E abi detaut, kega, Opole ma umele gaire lu uridili; a ma umele kaka mari lag. Iesu abi detager, kega, Kara mamoe giz darasisiare.
Ageakar, ageakar, kaka mari natager, kega, Ma makeriam emeret mabu eso, ma bakeam mabara lag: ma aule mabara tag nagisi, a nerute ko mari uanaso, a mari uanagared abele ma nole la kak.
E abele detager, abara tonar eud etomet Ade despili. E emetu abele detager, E ko abi detager, kega, Kari narmili.
Peteru egreamalu, a dasmer abele kaimeg Iesu nasge, E irmili ko; E dali Iesu ra marmot ge uteidilu ki ge eroare, a detager, kega, Opole, nete ko mari keserkeser?
Peteru abi dasmer, a Iesui detager, kega, Opole, E dali nako?
Iesu abi detager, kega, Ese kaka lagelag E kari naokaili, nako abele marim? ma kari narmili.
Abele mer ekoseli uiabim keimer giz, kega, Abele kaimeg le nole eud kak: Iesu nole abi detager, kega, Ma nole eud kak, epe, Ese kaka lagelag E kari naokaili, nako abele marim?
Abele kaimeg le E ageakarem abele gaire lu, a abele gaire lu detali: a meriba umele ageakar abara ageakar.
Dordor gaire uader lu Iesu de ikerare, ese detali uridili, kaka dikiapor nole abkoreb gesepem gaire jauali. Amen.
